<p>This is just the beginning, though; we'll keep working on providing a top-notch developer experience!</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/08/26/field-deprecation>Deprecation of the allow_message_deletion field</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-08-26T00:00:00.000Z>August 26, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>As of August 2025, we have updated the <code>team.preferences.list</code> API method to deprecate the <code>allow_message_deletion</code> response field. This field is no longer a preference, and will therefore no longer be returned from this API method. We'll be rolling out a permission to manage the ability to delete your own messages via the permissions page in the future, which will allow users to more granularly define who can delete their own messages on their team.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/deprecation>Deprecation</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/08/14/block-kit-table-block>Introducing the Block Kit table block!</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-08-14T00:00:00.000Z>August 14, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We've added a simpler way to display structured, tabular data in Slack: the Block Kit table block! Read more about how to implement this block in your app code <a class="" href=/reference/block-kit/blocks/table-block>here</a>.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/new-feature>New Feature</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/08/14/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v3.6.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-08-14T00:00:00.000Z>August 14, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>3.6.0</code> of the developer tools for the Slack platform is joining the summer fun!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">We added a new <code>runtime_not_found</code> error code that will appear when a hook script cannot be found because the runtime for a project wasn't found during execution.</li>
<li class="">We updated the <code>slack install</code> command to create and install new Bolt Framework apps that are configured to use app settings as the source of truth (i.e., remote manifest).</li>
<li class="">We updated the Slack CLI output to use the new tools URL at <a href=https://docs.slack.dev/tools target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">https://docs.slack.dev/tools</a> instead of the previous one at <a href=https://tools.slack.dev target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">https://tools.slack.dev</a>.</li>
<li class="">We added a <a href=https://downloads.slack-edge.com/slack-cli/slack_cli_latest_windows_64-bit.zip target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">download link</a> to the latest version of the Slack CLI for Windows. Manual installations for the latest are now also supported at the following links:<!-- -->
<ul>
<li class=""><a href=https://downloads.slack-edge.com/slack-cli/slack_cli_latest_linux_64-bit.tar.gz target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">https://downloads.slack-edge.com/slack-cli/slack_cli_latest_linux_64-bit.tar.gz</a></li>
<li class=""><a href=https://downloads.slack-edge.com/slack-cli/slack_cli_latest_macOS_arm64.tar.gz target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">https://downloads.slack-edge.com/slack-cli/slack_cli_latest_macOS_arm64.tar.gz</a></li>
<li class=""><a href=https://downloads.slack-edge.com/slack-cli/slack_cli_latest_macOS_amd64.tar.gz target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">https://downloads.slack-edge.com/slack-cli/slack_cli_latest_macOS_amd64.tar.gz</a></li>
<li class=""><a href=https://downloads.slack-edge.com/slack-cli/slack_cli_latest_macOS_64-bit.tar.gz target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">https://downloads.slack-edge.com/slack-cli/slack_cli_latest_macOS_64-bit.tar.gz</a></li>
<li class=""><a href=https://downloads.slack-edge.com/slack-cli/slack_cli_latest_windows_64-bit.zip target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">https://downloads.slack-edge.com/slack-cli/slack_cli_latest_windows_64-bit.zip</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug: we now allow new projects to be created more quickly by using a HTTP HEAD request to check whether the template URL exists.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug: we now order the outputs of authentication details from the <code>slack doctor</code> command according to an alphabetized list of team domains.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/07/31/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v3.5.2</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-07-31T00:00:00.000Z>July 31, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>3.5.2</code> of the developer tools for the Slack platform has landed!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Beginning <strong>September 1, 2025</strong>, the Slack CLI installation script will no longer include <code>deno</code> as part of the installation. We recommend installing <code>deno</code> separately and configuring CI systems as needed for app development (such as for <a href=https://docs.slack.dev/workflows/run-on-slack-infrastructure target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">ROSI</a> apps).</li>
<li class="">The <code>sdk_hook_not_found</code> error now provides a link to the Deno starter template <code>hooks.json</code> file as a working example.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/07/29/classic-apps-extension>Classic apps deprecation timeline adjustment</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-07-29T00:00:00.000Z>July 29, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We want to update you about our <a class="" href=/changelog/2024-09-legacy-custom-bots-classic-apps-deprecation>previous announcement</a> regarding support for classic apps. After much consideration and feedback, we have decided to push back the deprecation date to <strong>November 16, 2026</strong>.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/deprecation>Deprecation</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/07/21/featured-workflow-api>Introducing Slack Web API featured workflows</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-07-21T00:00:00.000Z>July 21, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>The Slack Web API featured workflows methods are now available! Use the <a class="" href=/reference/methods/workflows.featured.add><code>workflows.featured.add</code></a>, <a class="" href=/reference/methods/workflows.featured.list><code>workflows.featured.list</code></a>, <a class="" href=/reference/methods/workflows.featured.remove><code>workflows.featured.remove</code></a>, and <a class="" href=/reference/methods/workflows.featured.set><code>workflows.featured.set</code></a> methods to manage featured workflows programmatically.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/new-feature>New Feature</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/07/17/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v3.5.1</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-07-17T00:00:00.000Z>July 17, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>3.5.1</code> of the developer tools for the Slack platform is here!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">The install scripts now prompt you for feedback if an error occurs during the installation process.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/07/08/slack-marketplace>Installation requirement for Slack Marketplace apps</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-07-08T00:00:00.000Z>July 8, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We're making some changes to the entry requirements for apps submitting to the Slack Marketplace. Currently, we require that apps submitting to the Slack Marketplace have at least 10 installations on active workspaces. The goal behind this requirement is to ensure that all apps are thoroughly tested on a workspace other than the one they were built on. However, starting August 11th we will be reducing this requirement from 10 to 5 active workspaces! As part of this change, after this date we will automatically block submissions that don't meet this requirement. Please note: this requirement will not apply to apps that are already approved for the Slack Marketplace or submissions from apps that are not yet approved but are in the review process.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/07/03/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v3.5.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-07-03T00:00:00.000Z>July 3, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>3.5.0</code> of the developer tools for the Slack platform is here!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">The Bolt for JavaScript and Bolt for Python sample apps referenced in the documentation are now included in prompts of the <code>slack samples</code> command, and can be filtered using the <code>--language</code> flag.</li>
<li class="">Samples can now be created with a provided app name using the <code>slack samples</code> command with the provided app name.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug where the <code>slack run</code> command exited with an error if activity logs failed to stream. Now, retries are attempted for those missed logs.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/06/19/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v3.4.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-06-19T00:00:00.000Z>June 19, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>3.4.0</code> of the developer tools for the Slack platform is here!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">The install script and the <code>slack upgrade</code> command will now automatically detect your macOS architecture and install an Intel or an Apple Silicon binary.</li>
<li class="">Outputs from erroring hook scripts, such as those found when gathering an abnormal app manifest, are no longer hidden in verbose outputs but are instead shown with invocation errors.</li>
<li class="">In preparation for apps using the <a href=https://docs.slack.dev/workflows/run-on-slack-infrastructure target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Run on Slack infrastructure</a> to work with <a href=https://deno.com/blog/v2.0 target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Deno 2</a>, the following Deno ecosystem releases have gone out:<!-- -->
<ul>
<li class=""><code>v2.15.1</code> of the <a href=https://github.com/slackapi/deno-slack-sdk/releases/tag/2.15.1 target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Deno Slack SDK</a></li>
<li class=""><code>v1.4.0</code> of the <a href=https://github.com/slackapi/deno-slack-hooks/releases/tag/1.4.0 target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Deno Slack Hooks</a></li>
<li class=""><code>v1.1.3</code> of the <a href=https://github.com/slackapi/deno-slack-runtime/releases/tag/1.1.3 target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Deno Slack Runtime</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/06/05/api-site-sunsetting-update>Retiring of api.slack.com timeline adjustment</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-06-05T00:00:00.000Z>June 5, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We want to update you about our <a href=https://docs.slack.dev/changelog/2025/03/27/api-site-sunsetting target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">previous announcement</a> regarding the retirement of our old documentation experience on api.slack.com. We have moved the date from the end of <strong>June 2025</strong> to the end of <strong>August 2025</strong>.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/06/05/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v3.3.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-06-05T00:00:00.000Z>June 5, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>3.3.0</code> of the developer tools for the Slack platform has arrived!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">We've added native support for Apple silicon; the install script will use the matching <code>arm64</code> build for developers upgrading.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug when creating a project using a git repo template. Previously, if the template included <code>.git</code> within the URL, the template would fail to be cloned (for example, when running the <code>slack create --template https://github.com/slack-samples/example.git.project.git</code> command).</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug: setting the <code>source</code> using the flag for the <code>slack manifest info</code> command now takes precedence to project configurations, which are used to determine the default source.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/06/03/rate-limits-clarity>Clarifying rate limit changes for non-Marketplace apps</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-06-03T00:00:00.000Z>June 3, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We'd like to add additional clarity to the recent rate limits change for the <code>conversations.history</code> and <code>conversations.replies</code> Web API methods. Any internal customer-built apps will maintain their existing rate limits and will not be subject to the new posted limits. <a class="" href=/changelog/2025/05/29/rate-limit-changes-for-non-marketplace-apps>Read the updated FAQ for more info</a>, and please continue to reach out with questions!</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/05/29/rate-limit-changes-for-non-marketplace-apps>Rate limit changes for non-Marketplace apps</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-05-29T00:00:00.000Z>May 29, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class=admonitionHeading_Gvgb><span class=admonitionIcon_Rf37><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule=evenodd d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"/></svg></span><em>This page has been updated to clarify the rate limits for existing internal customer-built apps.</em></div></div>
<p>We're updating the rate limits for the <code>conversations.history</code> and <code>conversations.replies</code> Web API methods methods for non-Marketplace apps. This rate limit reduction will apply only to applications that are commercially distributed outside of the Marketplace (also called “unlisted” apps). It will immediately impact affect new unlisted applications and new installations of existing unlisted non-Marketplace applications. The new rate limits will be updated to allow 1 request per minute and will return a maximum of 15 objects per request.</p>
<p>The new rate limits will not be applied to existing installations of unlisted, distributed applications published outside the Marketplace.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Rate limit changes for non-Marketplace apps" href=/changelog/2025/05/29/rate-limit-changes-for-non-marketplace-apps><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/05/29/tos-updates>API Terms of Service updates</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-05-29T00:00:00.000Z>May 29, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We're making clarifications to the <a href=https://slack.com/terms-of-service/api target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">API Terms of Service</a> that will take effect immediately for new apps and on June 30, 2025 for existing apps. Please read the terms in full, but below is a summary of what’s changing:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Commercial Distribution:</strong> The updated terms confirm that the <a href=https://slack.com/marketplace target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Slack Marketplace</a> is the only appropriate channel for commercially distributing apps built with Slack APIs, whether those apps are unlisted (published outside of the Marketplace) or templatized one-off "custom" apps.</li>
<li class=""><strong>Data Usage Restrictions:</strong> We're reinforcing safeguards around how third-party applications can store, use, and share data accessed via Slack APIs.</li>
<li class=""><strong>API-Specific Terms:</strong> We're providing clearer guidance on how to use certain APIs, such as the Discovery API and the Real-Time Search API, responsibly.</li>
</ul>
<p>These updates strengthen and clarify existing Slack commitments to customers and are part of our ongoing effort to protect customer data, strengthen platform security, and ensure continued trust in the Slack ecosystem.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/05/22/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v3.2.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-05-22T00:00:00.000Z>May 22, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>3.2.0</code> of the developer tools for the Slack platform is here!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">We now display the manifest source as human-friendly output: <code>project (local)</code> and <code>app settings (remote)</code>. You'll see these changes in the <code>slack create</code>, <code>slack init</code>, and <code>slack app link &lt;id></code> commands, for example.</li>
<li class="">The link between your project code and the configurations within app settings can now be accessed by running the <code>slack app settings</code> command. Bolt developers with a remote manifest source managed within app settings may find this useful for discovering new features or making updates.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug: The example <code>slack app link</code> and <code>slack app list</code> commands shown when running the <code>slack app --help</code> command now use the entire command in order to prevent potential aliasing errors.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug to improve the console output to handle string values for versions.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/05/08/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v3.1.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-05-08T00:00:00.000Z>May 8, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>3.1.0</code> of the developer tools for the Slack platform has sprouted!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">We've updated the <code>slack app link</code> command to work with apps that have a <code>local</code> manifest source.</li>
<li class="">We've updated the <code>slack feedback</code> command to display a prompt for Slack CLI feedback: now you can ask questions, submit issues, or suggest features for the Slack CLI through GitHub Issues.</li>
<li class="">Related to the above update, the <code>slack feedback --name platform-improvements</code> command has been replaced with <code>slack feedback --name slack-platform</code>. You can continue to use the <code>--name platform-improvements</code> flag until the next major version release.</li>
<li class="">We updated the <code>slack feedback</code> command error message to account for a missing <code>--name &lt;id></code> flag and to clarify that the name is specified as a flag. You should now see: <em>Please provide a <code>--name</code> flag or remove the <code>--no-prompt</code> flag</em>.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug with a rare edge case that caused the Slack CLI to hang without exiting the process. Now, the Slack CLI will exit with the correct error code and allow sub-processes to clean up.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/04/24/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v3.0.5</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-04-24T00:00:00.000Z>April 24, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>3.0.5</code> of the developer tools for the Slack platform has bloomed!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">The Slack CLI and installation scripts now point to our new Slack platform documentation at <a href=https://docs.slack.dev/ target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">docs.slack.dev</a> and our developer tools documentation at <a href=https://tools.slack.dev/ target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">tools.slack.dev</a>.</li>
<li class="">As part of the <a href=https://docs.slack.dev/changelog/2025/04/10/slack-cli-goes-open-source target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Slack CLI going open source</a>, the Slack CLI documentation has gone open source as well!</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug: When running the <code>slack upgrade</code> command inside a project directory, the output now notes whether the latest SDK versions were checked.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/04/11/classic-apps-extension>Classic apps deprecation timeline adjustment</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-04-11T00:00:00.000Z>April 11, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We want to update you about our <a class="" href=/changelog/2024-09-legacy-custom-bots-classic-apps-deprecation>previous announcement</a> regarding support for classic apps. After much consideration and feedback, we have decided to push back the deprecation date to <strong>May 25, 2026</strong>.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/deprecation>Deprecation</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/04/10/slack-cli-goes-open-source>The Slack CLI is now open source!</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-04-10T00:00:00.000Z>April 10, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Long a staple of apps built with the Deno Slack SDK—and now with recent support for the Bolt framework—we're proud to make the ever-growing Slack CLI part of our collection of open source tooling.</p>
<p>We love contributions from our community, so we encourage you to explore and interact with the <a href=https://github.com/slackapi/slack-cli target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">GitHub repo</a>. Contributions, bug reports, and any feedback are all helpful; let us nurture the Slack CLI together to help make building Slack apps more pleasant for everyone.</p>
<p>Not familiar with the Slack CLI? Visit the docs and follow the <a class="" href=/tools/slack-cli/guides/installing-the-slack-cli-for-mac-and-linux/>installation guide</a> to begin your journey.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/04/10/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v3.0.4</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-04-10T00:00:00.000Z>April 10, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>3.0.4</code> of the developer tools for the Slack platform is here!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">We fixed a bug: we updated the URL in the <code>hooks.json</code> error message to use a working, valid URL.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/03/27/api-site-sunsetting>Retiring of api.slack.com</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-03-27T00:00:00.000Z>March 27, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>As <a href=https://docs.slack.dev/changelog/2025/03/10/api-site-migration-launch target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">previously announced</a>, the Slack platform and developer tools documentation are moving: the Slack platform documentation is now in beta on <a href=https://docs.slack.dev/ target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">docs.slack.dev</a>, and the developer tools documentation has moved to its new home on <a href=https://tools.slack.dev/ target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">tools.slack.dev</a>.</p>
<p>Our next step is to sunset the old documentation experience on api.slack.com, and we plan to do so by the end of <del>June</del> <strong>August 2025</strong>. In the meantime, you may want to update any bookmarks you have pointing to api.slack.com—but not to worry, we'll have redirects in place to make sure you end up right where you need to be!</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/03/27/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v3.0.2</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-03-27T00:00:00.000Z>March 27, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>3.0.2</code> of the developer tools for the Slack platform is here!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">We've updated the <code>slack version</code> command to include additional descriptive information and examples when using the <code>--help</code> flag.</li>
<li class="">We've updated the feedback URL when using the <code>slack feedback</code> command to point to the home of our new and improved documentation on <a href=https://docs.slack.dev/ target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">docs.slack.dev</a>!</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/03/19/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v3.0.1</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-03-19T00:00:00.000Z>March 19, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Slack CLI <code>v3.0.1</code> delivers a handful of small improvements thanks to our developer community feedback.</p>
<ul>
<li class="">We've fixed the <code>--token</code> flag and it'll work when combined with the <code>--app</code> and <code>--team</code> flags.</li>
<li class="">We've fixed the <code>--app</code> flag to use the specified app and it'll work when combined with the <code>--team</code> flag.</li>
<li class="">We've disabled app manifest caching and overwrite protection for Deno Slack SDK apps that run on Slack because it's not required.</li>
<li class="">We've fixed a bug to support large manifest files by allowing the hooks to parse multi-line boundaries.</li>
<li class="">We've fixed a bug to prevent creating a new app that would overwrite an existing app for a specified team.</li>
<li class="">We've fixed a bug to show an app's team name and team ID, when the app's auth is missing.</li>
<li class="">We've fixed a bug to reset terminal text formatting after prompts, which conflicts with tools such as Python virtual environments.</li>
<li class="">We've improved the performance of resolving the authentication for local, dev apps by reducing the reading of your credentials file.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/03/17/files-upload-extension>files.upload API method deprecation timeline adjustment</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-03-17T00:00:00.000Z>March 17, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We want to update you about our <a href=https://docs.slack.dev/changelog/2024-04-a-better-way-to-upload-files-is-here-to-stay target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">previous announcement</a> regarding support for the <code>files.upload</code> API method. After much consideration and feedback, we have decided to push back the deprecation date to <strong>November 12, 2025</strong>.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/deprecation>Deprecation</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>Breaking change</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/03/10/api-site-migration-launch>Slack platform API and tools docs are now in beta</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-03-10T00:00:00.000Z>March 10, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Today is the day! As <a href=https://docs.slack.dev/changelog/2024/12/05/api-site-migration target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">previously mentioned</a>, the Slack platform and developer tools documentation are moving: the shiny new Slack platform documentation is now in beta on <a href=https://docs.slack.dev/ target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">docs.slack.dev</a>, and the developer tools documentation has fully moved to its new home on <a href=https://tools.slack.dev/ target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">tools.slack.dev</a>. The doors are open for our housewarming party 🥳 so come on in, take a look around, and let us know what you think. Thanks for coming along on this journey with us!</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/02/27/slack-cli-release>Release: Slack CLI v3.0.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-02-27T00:00:00.000Z>February 27, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>3.0.0</code> of the developer tools for the Slack automations platform is here, with lots of goodies for you!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">We renamed the <code>slack.json</code> file to <code>.slack/hooks.json</code>, and continue to support <code>slack.json</code> for existing projects. There is now a warning shown in <code>--verbose</code> output to encourage projects to migrate their <code>slack.json</code> to <code>.slack/hooks.json.</code></li>
<li class="">We've removed the <code>invalid_app_directory</code> error from any commands run in nested project directories, and now search for the required <code>slack.json</code> file in the project's configuration. We also now also check for this file at <code>.slack/hooks.json</code>.</li>
<li class="">We now cache the last known manifest export; the cache is used to avoid overwriting changes on app settings. If the manifest is changed on app settings since the last update, a confirmation prompt will appear before making another update via the Slack CLI.</li>
<li class="">We've moved the top-level commands you know and love, <code>slack create</code> and <code>slack samples</code>, to be sub-commands of the <code>slack project</code> command (they remain aliased as top-level commands though, so there is no change to the user experience).</li>
<li class="">We've updated the <code>slack doctor</code> command to display the <code>manifest.source</code> value, which will be either <code>local</code> or <code>remote</code>.</li>
<li class="">We now officially support Bolt for JavaScript and Bolt for Python in the Slack CLI! 🎉</li>
<li class="">As such, we've updated the <code>slack create</code> command with a new create journey that allows you to choose between different types of apps for Bolt for JavaScript, Bolt for Python, and Deno.</li>
<li class="">We've also added the <code>slack init</code> command, which will initialize an existing Bolt for JavaScript, Bolt for Python, or Deno project with Slack CLI support.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug to avoid confusion with regular outputs, and now prefix all separate debug logs with a timestamp.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug to avoid spinning the spinner when outputting with debug logs, or if styles are removed with the <code>--no-color</code> flag.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug to now display uninstalled apps in selections when using the <code>slack collaborators</code> and <code>slack manifest</code> commands.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug with confirming trusted templates that are from a Slack GitHub organization.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug regarding writing console outputs to activity logs during local runs.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug where the Slack CLI would get stuck if one of the goroutines of the <code>slack run</code> command encountered an error; we now exit the <code>slack run</code> command if this happens.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/02/27/slack-cli>Removing the Slack CLI deno command</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-02-27T00:00:00.000Z>February 27, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We <a class="" href=/changelog/2023/12/14/slack-cli>previously</a> mentioned that we had deprecated the <code>deno</code> command and removed its listing from the <code>help</code> command. We have now removed the <code>deno</code> command completely. Developers who were depending on this command should now use the deno executable directly.</p>
<p>We've also removed support for the deprecated, pre-release Deno Slack SDK versions that used <code>slack.yaml</code> and <code>project.ts</code> files. The Run-on-Slack platform no longer supports the <code>slack.yaml</code> file format, and no production projects should be affected. The <code>project.ts</code> file was deprecated by the Deno Slack SDK in favor of <code>manifest.ts</code> and <code>manifest.json</code> files.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>Breaking change</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/02/13/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v2.33</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-02-13T00:00:00.000Z>February 13, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>2.33.0</code> of the developer tools for the Slack automations platform will be your valentine!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">We now support running CLI commands in project sub-directories.</li>
<li class="">We've enhanced the script and outputs of hooks to improve debugging.</li>
<li class="">We've fixed a bug to properly output error messages that may occur when the <code>slack manifest</code> command is run.</li>
<li class="">We've fixed a bug to distinguish between Slack CLI names if your Slack CLI is named something other than <code>slack</code>.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/02/03/block-kit-markdown>A new Block Kit block is now available for use!</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-02-03T00:00:00.000Z>February 3, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>The <a class="" href=/reference/block-kit/blocks#markdown>markdown block</a> for <a class="" href=/block-kit>Block Kit</a> accepts standard markdown and outputs formatted Slack markdown; intended for use in <a class="" href=/ai/developing-agents>apps that use platform AI features</a>.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/new-feature>New Feature</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/01/30/data-access-api>The Data Access API is here!</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-01-30T00:00:00.000Z>January 30, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>This API is now available in a limited release for interested partners. Use the <a class="" href=/apis/web-api/real-time-search-api>Data Access API</a> within apps that have the Agents & AI Apps feature enabled to access all the relevant Slack data you need to ensure a pleasant user experience for AI-enabled apps</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/new-feature>New Feature</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2025/01/16/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v2.32.1</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2025-01-16T00:00:00.000Z>January 16, 2025</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>2.32.1</code> of the developer tools for the Slack automations platform has arrived!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">
<p>In the Deno Slack Hooks <code>1.3.2</code> release, we've improved the bundling used for the <code>slack deploy</code> command to address some issued encountered with <code>npm</code> imports.</p>
</li>
<li class="">
<p>We fixed a bug to skip the hosted app pre-run check when the <code>--force</code> flag is used.</p>
</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2024/12/12/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v2.32.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2024-12-12T00:00:00.000Z>December 12, 2024</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>2.32.0</code> of the developer tools for the Slack automations platform is here!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">We improved detection of <a class="" href=/tools/deno-slack-sdk/guides/installing-deno>Deno</a> projects and added test coverage to the Deno runtime for a smoother experience.</li>
<li class="">We improved the formatting of output when running <code>slack env</code> commands. We also added error messaging to these commands when the app being referenced is not an app created using the Deno Slack SDK.</li>
<li class="">The <code>slack env remove</code> command now exits without erroring when there are no environment variables to remove.</li>
<li class="">We enhanced text styling for easier reading.</li>
<li class="">We improved some internal processes that allow us to keep our documentation fresh and up-to-date.</li>
<li class="">We improved the error messaging of our <code>slack datastore</code> commands.</li>
<li class="">We updated our documentation and errors displayed when using <code>slack external-auth</code> subcommands with Bolt apps.</li>
<li class="">We now raise errors that may impact the validation of selected authentications.</li>
<li class="">We now hide blank <code>source</code> errors that may have caused confusion; they have been replaced with more helpful messaging.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2024/12/10/dev-policy-update>Slack App Developer Policy updates</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2024-12-10T00:00:00.000Z>December 10, 2024</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>On <strong>December 10, 2024</strong>, we updated the <a class="" href=/developer-policy>Slack App Developer Policy</a> to add clarity to guidance from our documentation that apps intended for commercial distribution at scale should go through Slack Marketplace review.</p>
<p>While gathering feedback from early customers helps improve your apps, the Slack Marketplace is the right place for apps as they begin to grow. The Slack Marketplace guidelines and our review process help keep the Slack app ecosystem working and customer data secure.</p>
<p>We also clarified existing guidelines about the usage of data collected by your app. Specifically, we are making explicit that the use of data to train an LLM is prohibited.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Slack App Developer Policy updates" href=/changelog/2024/12/10/dev-policy-update><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2024/12/05/api-site-migration>Slack platform API and tools docs are moving</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2024-12-05T00:00:00.000Z>December 5, 2024</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>As you may have read in our November newsletter, Slack platform API documentation is moving! The Slack Documentation team is currently overhauling the API documentation—both front-end and back-end—to enhance your developer documentation experience.</p>
<p>While you won’t see any changes until <strong>March 2025</strong>, we promise to keep you in the loop. Change is a journey, and we’re here with you every step of the way!</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Slack platform API and tools docs are moving" href=/changelog/2024/12/05/api-site-migration><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2024/11/14/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v2.31.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2024-11-14T00:00:00.000Z>November 14, 2024</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version 2.31.0 of the developer tools for the Slack automations platform has landed!</p>
<p>We fixed a bug that would display errors when the <code>slack run</code> command was interrupted during app selection. The fix also includes an <code>org_grant_exists</code> error, which is raised if an attempt is made to grant installation permission to another workspace when your app has already been granted one.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2024/11/07/apps>Classic apps deprecation timeline adjustment</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2024-11-07T00:00:00.000Z>November 7, 2024</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We want to update you about our <a class="" href=/changelog/2024-09-legacy-custom-bots-classic-apps-deprecation>previous announcement</a> regarding support for classic apps. After much consideration and feedback, we have decided to push back the deprecation date for classic apps to <strong>March 31, 2026</strong>.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/deprecation>Deprecation</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2024/10/31/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v2.30.1</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2024-10-31T00:00:00.000Z>October 31, 2024</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Boo! Version 2.30.1 of the developer tools for the Slack automations platform has sneaked up behind you.</p>
<p>We fixed a bug such that expired tokens will now be removed from your local credentials, and the <code>token_expired</code> error will be logged when debugging if returned when using the <code>slack logout</code> command. No tricks, only treats!</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2024/10/17/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v2.30.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2024-10-17T00:00:00.000Z>October 17, 2024</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version 2.30.0 of the developer tools for the Slack automations platform has spookily appeared!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">We added some behind the scenes CLI support for <a class="" href=/ai>Agents & AI Apps</a>.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug such that app manifest validation when running <code>slack deploy</code> now respects use of the <code>--force</code> flag. We also fixed a few other bugs related to app manifest validation to make things run more smoothly.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug such that running the <code>slack create</code> command will use either the absolute or relative path provided when creating your app.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2024-09-legacy-custom-bots-classic-apps-deprecation>Discontinuing support for legacy custom bots and classic apps</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2024-09-30T00:00:00.000Z>September 30, 2024</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We want to let you know about some upcoming changes to support for legacy custom bots and classic apps on the Slack platform.</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Beginning <strong>March 31, 2025</strong>, we will discontinue support for legacy custom bots. For your integrations to continue working, you must create brand new Slack apps.</li>
<li class="">
<s>In <strong>September 2025</strong> <strong>March 2026</strong> <strong>May 2026</strong> <strong>November 2026</strong>, we will discontinue support for classic apps. For your apps to continue working, you will need to <a class="" href=/legacy/legacy-app-migration/migrating-classic-apps>migrate them to Slack apps</a>. Any custom bots or classic apps you have built will no longer work after these dates.</s>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class=admonitionHeading_Gvgb><span class=admonitionIcon_Rf37><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule=evenodd d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"/></svg></span>Classic apps deprecation has been paused</div><div class=admonitionContent_BuS1><p>We have paused any changes relating to classic apps at this time. Classic apps will continue to work, but we recommend migrating them to Slack apps to take advantage of their benefits.</div></div>
<p>It has been over 10 years since we originally launched the Slack Platform. As we <a class="" href=/changelog/2024-04-discontinuing-new-creation-of-classic-slack-apps-and-custom-bots>mentioned back in April 2024</a>, there are just too many ways to create an app, so we're doing our best to streamline this process.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/deprecation>Deprecation</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>Breaking change</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Discontinuing support for legacy custom bots and classic apps" href=/changelog/2024-09-legacy-custom-bots-classic-apps-deprecation><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2024/09/16/apps>Agents & AI Apps feature is here!</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2024-09-16T00:00:00.000Z>September 16, 2024</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We're excited to announce that the following new features have launched!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Introducing the <a class="" href=/ai>Agents & AI Apps</a> feature, the new way you can build AI-powered, conversational apps integrated with your favorite Large Language Model (LLM).</li>
<li class="">The App Directory is now the <a class="" href=/slack-marketplace>Slack Marketplace</a>! Get ready to explore a whole new world of apps, assistants, templates, connectors, and more.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/new-feature>New feature</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2024/09/05/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v2.29.2</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2024-09-05T00:00:00.000Z>September 5, 2024</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version 2.29.2 of the developer tools for the Slack automations platform is hot off the press!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">When logging into a project directory using the <code>slack login</code> command, the Slack CLI will now suggest also running the <code>slack app list</code> command. When logging in outside of a project directory, the Slack CLI will continue to suggest running the <code>slack create</code> command to create a new project.</li>
<li class="">We've fixed some bugs behind the curtain and added some CI/CD improvements.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2024/08/14/apps>Custom workflow steps for all Slack apps are available today!</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2024-08-14T00:00:00.000Z>August 14, 2024</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Refer to <a class="" href=/workflows/workflow-steps>workflow steps</a> and <a class="" href=/workflows/workflow-steps>custom steps for Bolt apps</a> for more details.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/new-feature>New feature</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2024/08/08/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v2.29.1</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2024-08-08T00:00:00.000Z>August 8, 2024</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version 2.29.1 of the developer tools for the Slack automations platform has arrived!</p>

<ul>
<li class="">You can now update your local project's <code>apps.json</code> file with app IDs for your existing apps using the <code>slack app link</code> command. Refer to <a class="" href=/tools/slack-cli/reference/commands/slack_app>app commands</a> for more details.</li>
<li class="">We've updated the formatting for section text and trace prints for the <code>slack collaborator add</code>, <code>slack collaborator list</code>, and <code>slack collaborator remove</code> commands.</li>
<li class="">We've updated the debug log output when installing dependencies using the <code>slack create</code> command. We also now suggest installing project dependencies if an error occurs when running this command.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug to avoid formatting printed strings if the string to be printed has no arguments.</li>
<li class="">We now set authentication configurations such as custom API hosts for selected tokens with the <code>slack manifest validate</code> command.</li>
<li class="">Starting <strong>June 11, 2024</strong>, we are enforcing admin restrictions on built-in steps and webhook triggers in coded workflows. This update aims to align the security settings of coded workflows with those of connector steps and triggers. Read on to learn more.</li>

<li class="">We now display a more informative message when you attempt to delete or uninstall an app from a project that has no apps.</li>

Refer to <a class="" href=/tools/deno-slack-sdk/guides/creating-event-triggers#scoping>scoping channel-based event triggers</a> for more details.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/deno-slack-api>Deno Slack API</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/deno-slack-sdk>Deno Slack SDK</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2024-04-a-better-way-to-upload-files-is-here-to-stay>The files.upload method is retiring, to be replaced by sequenced Web API methods</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2024-04-09T11:00:00.000Z>April 9, 2024</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>The original web API method for uploading files to Slack, <a class="" href=/reference/methods/files.upload><code>files.upload</code></a>, is being sunset on <s><strong>March 11, 2025</strong></s> <strong>November 12, 2025</strong>.</p>
<p>As of <strong>May 16, 2024</strong>, newly-created apps are no longer able to use this API method.</p>
<p>Existing apps & integrations should migrate away from <code>files.upload</code> and instead leverage a combination of two APIs: <a class="" href=/reference/methods/files.getUploadURLExternal><code>files.getUploadURLExternal</code></a> and <a class="" href=/reference/methods/files.completeUploadExternal><code>files.completeUploadExternal</code></a>. The use of these two methods is more reliable, especially when uploading large files.</p>
<p>A detailed breakdown of how to use these two API methods is described in our <a class="" href=/messaging/working-with-files#uploading_files>Uploading files documentation</a>.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/deprecation>Deprecation</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>breaking change</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about The files.upload method is retiring, to be replaced by sequenced Web API methods" href=/changelog/2024-04-a-better-way-to-upload-files-is-here-to-stay><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2024/04/04/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v2.21.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2024-04-04T00:00:00.000Z>April 4, 2024</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>2.21.0</code> of the developer tools for the Slack automations platform has sprung!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">You can now display runtime versions for your application's execution environment using the <code>doctor</code> hook. To enjoy the improved <code>slack doctor</code> command experience, existing Deno Slack SDK-based apps must have their <code>deno-slack-hooks</code> dependency upgraded to the latest version (<code>v1.3.0</code>).</li>
<li class="">By relying only on the <code>get-manifest</code> hook when attempting to get a manifest rather than checking for a <code>slack.yaml</code> file, we now surface any errors that are returned when getting the manifest.</li>
<li class="">We removed the possibility of an error when generating the message boundary hook protocol, and now preserve spacing in logged outputs.</li>
<li class="">We corrected a few typos behind the scenes.</li>

<p>use:</p>

<li class="">Users can now request app approval at the workspace level in an Enterprise organization.</li>
<li class="">We now include the error code in event payloads to logstash.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug to output a link if opening the URL in a browser fails.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug to catch missing hooks from a command; the initialization error is now included in the debug outputs. This allows any command to be run from a project directory without immediately posting an error.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug to remove ANSI escape sequences from the debug log outputs for an improved grepping experience.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug to verify that deprecated flags are properly substituted.</li>
<li class="">We fixed an issue to make our releases run more smoothly. Nothing to see here!</li>

<ul>
<li class="">The minimum supported PowerShell version as of this release is <code>v6.0</code>. If you attempt to use an older version of PowerShell, you may encounter errors reading the Slack Configuration file (<code>slack.json</code>) or running the <code>get hooks</code> hook.</li>
<li class="">We've added the ability to put, get, and delete items in bulk in a datastore. Refer to <a class="" href=/tools/deno-slack-sdk/guides/adding-items-to-a-datastore>Create or replace items with <code>put</code> and <code>bulkPut</code></a>, <a class="" href=/tools/deno-slack-sdk/guides/retrieving-items-from-a-datastore>Retrieve items with <code>get</code> and <code>bulkGet</code></a>, and <a class="" href=/tools/deno-slack-sdk/guides/deleting-items-from-a-datastore>Delete items with <code>delete</code> and <code>bulkDelete</code></a>, respectively.</li>

<li class="">We've added a warning when creating an app from a sample app when the sample app may not have come from a trusted source.</li>
<li class="">You can disable this warning temporarily by running the <code>slack create</code> command with the <code>--force</code> flag.</li>
<li class="">You can disable this warning permanently by either selecting <em>don't ask again</em> when prompted, or by setting the <code>trust_unknown_sources</code> property in your <code>config.json</code> file.</li>
<li class="">We've fixed an issue so can now use <strong>CTRL-C</strong> to unhide your cursor when a spinner displays after running <code>slack deploy</code>.</li>
<li class="">We've enhanced some error messages and we've improved highlighting matching for help commands.</li>

<ul>
<li class="">We've updated the <em>choose a workspace to grant access</em> prompt to sort by team name rather than team ID.</li>
<li class="">We've deprecated the <code>deno</code> command and removed its listing from the <code>help</code> command. The <code>deno</code> command is slated to be removed completely in an upcoming release.</li>
<li class="">Endpoints at <code>api.slack.com</code> are no longer blocked by a permission error for local apps.</li>
<li class="">We now have better error handling when appending a <code>(local)</code> tag to the display name of local apps.</li>
<li class="">We've removed some extra blank lines and debug information from command outputs for a cleaner look and faster feel.</li>
<li class="">We've provided prompts for possible trigger IDs for trigger commands that need them.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023/11/30/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v2.14.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-11-30T00:00:00.000Z>November 30, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>2.14.0</code> of the developer tools for the Slack automations platform is here!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">We've updated the CLI to prompt you to request admin approval for an Admin-Approved App using a connector function that is not currently approved for use in your workspace. For more information, refer to <a class="" href=/tools/deno-slack-sdk/guides/controlling-permissions-for-admins>Platform permissions control for admins</a>.</li>
<li class="">We've formatted the system and project configs with indents to make editing easier.</li>
<li class="">We've added a <code>SLACK_CONFIG_DIR</code> environment variable to the <code>--config-dir</code> global flag.</li>
<li class="">The <code>uninstall</code> command is now available from the list displayed when using the <code>--help</code> flag.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023/11/16/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v2.13.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-11-16T00:00:00.000Z>November 16, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>2.13.0</code> of the developer tools for the Slack automations platform has landed!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">We've added an <code>--all-org-workspace-grants</code> flag to the <code>app list</code> command so you can display all grants instead of only the first three.</li>
<li class="">We've combined <code>workspace</code> and <code>org</code> language into <code>team</code>; as such, we have added a <code>--team</code> flag and deprecated the <code>--workspace</code> flag. Note that this will not affect the usage of workspace or org when it is necessary to distinguish between them; for example, with the <code>hermes auth list</code> and <code>trigger access</code> commands.</li>
<li class="">We removed the redirect to the <code>delete</code> command when running the <code>uninstall</code> command, so you may now only uninstall an app rather than deleting the app entirely along with all of its data.</li>
<li class="">We've updated the CLI installer to align the Deno runtime version with the current version supported by the Slack platform.</li>
<li class="">We've updated all <code>deno-reverse-string</code> sample app references to use <code>deno-started-template</code> instead.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug to create a <code>usr/local/bin</code> directory if it is missing when installing the CLI.</li>
<li class="">We updated some confusing language related to breaking changes.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug that caused an error when any property setting flags were provided along with the <code>--trigger-def</code> flag.</li>
<li class="">We fixed a bug where descriptions and selected template URLs might be mismatched from the displayed list of samples.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023/11/06/apis>SCIM API token restriction by IP address</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-11-06T00:00:00.000Z>November 6, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Keep your user data secret and safe.
