<ul>
<li class="">We've improved Deno dependency caching.</li>
<li class="">The <code>app list</code> command no longer requires authentication, and will instead display an <code>unknown</code> app status in cases where no authentication is found.</li>
<li class="">The <code>run</code>, <code>deploy</code>, and <code>delete</code> commands will now resolve organization-level authentication in cases where workspace-level authentication is missing.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023-08-workflow-steps-from-apps-step-back>Workflow Steps from Apps step back</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-08-22T11:00:00.000Z>August 22, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We're retiring support for traditional Slack apps providing <em>Steps from Apps</em> to our legacy workflow builder and workflows created with it. Read on to learn whether your apps or workflows are impacted.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>Breaking change</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/deprecation>Deprecation</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Workflow Steps from Apps step back" href=/changelog/2023-08-workflow-steps-from-apps-step-back><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023/08/10/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v2.7.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-08-10T00:00:00.000Z>August 10, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>2.7.0</code> of the developer tools for the Slack automations platform has arrived!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">We've added a <a class="" href=/tools/slack-cli/reference/commands/slack_trigger_list><code>slack trigger list --type=&lt;string></code></a> flag to only list triggers of a specific type: For example, <code>slack trigger list --type=shortcut</code>. We've also supported flag values for <code>--type=&lt;string></code> are <code>all</code>, <code>shortcut</code>, <code>event</code>, <code>webhook</code>, <code>scheduled</code>, and <code>external</code>.</li>
<li class="">We've added flags to provide values for many interactive prompts. Learn more about the flags available by adding <code>--help</code> to any command. For example, <code>slack external-auth add-secret --provider github --secret my-secret-value</code>.</li>
<li class="">We've updated the <code>slack app list</code> command to improve displaying apps you are not authenticated to access. For example, local apps now display a <code>(local)</code> label and install status is now shown as <code>Status: Unknown</code>.</li>
<li class="">We removed an incorrect timestamp found in the Slack debug log file.</li>
<li class="">The Deno Slack SDK v2.2.0 now displays an error in your editor when you accidentally register duplicate primary keys for <code>workflow</code>, <code>function</code>, <code>datastore</code>, <code>customType</code>, <code>event</code> or <code>provider</code>. This helps prevent unexpected behavior at runtime.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023/08/01/apps>Slack Marketplace submissions must now have a minimum of 10 active workspace installations to be reviewed</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-08-01T00:00:00.000Z>August 1, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p><a class="" href=/slack-marketplace/slack-marketplace-app-guidelines-and-requirements#suitable>Read more in our submission guidelines.</a></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023-07-its-later-already-for-stars-and-reminders>It's later already for stars and reminders</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-07-31T00:00:00.000Z>July 31, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Starting in March 2023, Slack began rolling out a new collection of features collectively called <a href=https://slack.com/help/articles/13453851074067-Save-it-for-Later target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class=""><strong><em>Save it for Later</em></strong></a>. It gives you a new <strong><em>Later</em></strong> section on Slack where things you save for later (with or without a reminder attached to it) are kept.</p>
<p>This new collection of features replaces our previous <strong><em>Saved Items</em></strong> (also known as <em>starred items</em>, or just <em>stars</em>) and <strong><em>Reminders</em></strong> features.</p>
<p>As part of this new feature roll out, the existing APIs to interface with saved items and reminders have become degraded or useless. There are no direct APIs for <strong><em>Save it for Later</em></strong> to integrate with. With the current suite of built-in functions, web API methods, events, and triggers offered by Slack it is possible to recreate some (but certainly not all) use cases the impacted APIs supported.</p>
<p>We aim to give ample notice for every platform feature developers would consider a “breaking change.” We apologize we were unable to provide this information to developers ahead of the <strong><em>Save it for Later</em></strong> release.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/deprecation>Deprecation</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>Breaking change</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about It's later already for stars and reminders" href=/changelog/2023-07-its-later-already-for-stars-and-reminders><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023/07/27/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v2.6.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-07-27T00:00:00.000Z>July 27, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>2.6.0</code> of the developer tools for the Slack automations platform has arrived!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">The <code>.github</code> directory will no longer be included in new projects created from one of our <a href=https://github.com/slack-samples target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">sample apps</a>.</li>
<li class="">The <code>slack app list</code> command now returns <code>Status: Installed</code> instead of <code>Status: Unknown</code> for an installed app.</li>
<li class="">When using the CLI in a non-interactive environment, such as in a CI pipeline, selection prompts will error and suggest a flag alternative to use instead of hanging indefinitely.</li>
<li class="">Trigger generation prompts will be automatically skipped when using <code>slack run</code> or <code>slack deploy</code> in a non-interactive environment, regardless of how many triggers might exist.</li>
<li class="">We've clarified admin approval requirements when installing to a workspace that has <a class="" href=/tools/deno-slack-sdk/guides/controlling-permissions-for-admins>Admin-Approved Apps</a> enabled.</li>
<li class="">Socket connections are now gracefully closed when ending a <code>slack run</code> session.</li>
<li class="">Improved typeahead suggestions for the <code>type</code> field of <code>functions</code> and <code>datastores</code> were made in the Deno Slack SDK.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023/07/10/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v2.5.1</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-07-10T00:00:00.000Z>July 10, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>2.5.1</code> fixes a bug to now properly delete the selected app when uninstalling it from a workspace.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023/06/29/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v2.5.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-06-29T00:00:00.000Z>June 29, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>2.5.0</code> of the developer tools for the Slack automations platform is hot off the press!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">We've added a confirmation message if you decide not to delete an app when using the <code>slack app delete</code> command.</li>
<li class="">We added a <code>--hide-triggers</code> flag to the <code>slack run</code> and <code>slack deploy</code> commands to prevent retrieving and displaying application triggers.</li>
<li class="">We added a warning to listed trigger info that Slack Connect channels do not support event triggers.</li>
<li class="">We added app collaborators to listed trigger info.</li>
<li class="">We added support to limit paginated results with the <code>trigger list --limit &lt;n></code> command.</li>
<li class="">We added a prompt for whether you would like to include/exclude app collaborators into the named entities list if you set your trigger's ACL to <code>named_entities</code>. The <code>include-app-collaborators</code> flag will allow you to skip this prompt.</li>
<li class="">We updated the <code>slack activity</code> command to support datastore event and error logs. For more information, refer to <a class="" href=/tools/deno-slack-sdk/guides/logging-function-and-app-behavior>logging</a>.</li>
<li class="">When the <code>--token</code> flag is set, background checks for updates will now be automatically disabled.</li>
<li class="">We added support to fall back to a <code>curl</code> install of <code>deno</code> if <code>deno upgrade</code> should fail.</li>
<li class="">The <code>slack logout</code> command now accepts the <code>--workspace</code> flag.</li>
<li class="">We removed the <code>--show-triggers</code> flag from the <code>slack run</code> command, as the command now displays all of your app's triggers and their types.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023/06/28/slack-cli>Slack CLI v1.17.0 and below is now deprecated</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-06-28T00:00:00.000Z>June 28, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Beginning <strong>June 28, 2023</strong>, version <code>v1.17.0</code> and below of the CLI is deprecated. We recommend reinstalling the CLI to get the latest version. <a class="" href=/tools/deno-slack-sdk/guides/getting-started>Learn more</a>.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/deprecation>Deprecation</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023/06/15/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v2.4.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-06-15T00:00:00.000Z>June 15, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>2.4.0</code> of the developer tools for the Slack automations platform is now available!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">We updated the Linux/macOS installation script to support a CLI version param, <code>-v</code>.</li>
<li class="">We added a <code>-d</code> flag to bypass Deno installation in the Linux/macOS installation script.</li>
<li class="">We updated the Windows installation script to include Alias, Version, SkipDeno, and SkipGit flags.</li>
<li class="">We now suggest Windows users open a new terminal after installation to add the Slack CLI to the user's environment PATH.</li>
<li class="">We bumped minimum required Deno version to <code>1.31.1</code>.</li>
<li class="">We replaced the <code>workspace</code> command with a new <a class="" href=/tools/slack-cli/reference/commands/slack_app><code>app</code></a> command.</li>
<li class="">We made the <code>config-dir</code> global flag visible.</li>
<li class="">We deprecated auth login's <code>auth</code> flag in favor of <a class="" href=/tools/slack-cli/reference/commands/slack_auth_login><code>token</code></a>.</li>
<li class="">We updated <code>app list</code> command to display installation status.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023/06/01/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v2.3.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-06-01T00:00:00.000Z>June 1, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>2.3.0</code> of the developer tools for the Slack automations platform has arrived!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">The <code>external-auth remove</code> command now allows you to select a token for deletion.</li>
<li class="">The new <code>external-auth select-auth</code> command allows you to select a unique auth for each of the workflows in an app. This command is mandatory when using new coded workflows that have a step containing <code>credentialSource DEVELOPER</code>; that is, every time a coded workflow is created, this command must be called after the <code>external-auth add</code> command.</li>
<li class="">The <code>slack auth token</code> and <code>slack auth revoke</code> commands allow you to manage service tokens.</li>
<li class="">The <code>slack auth token</code> command allows you to get the <code>slackauthticket</code> and copy and paste it into your workspace to exchange for the service token. The service token will not be saved to your <code>credentials.json</code> file; instead, it is presented in the prompt for you to copy and paste to your CI/CD pipelines. Once you obtained a service token, you can use the <code>slack login --auth &lt;your-service-token></code> command to authorize your Slack CLI. The service token will not conflict with your regular authentication token; you can continue using your regular authentication token within the Slack CLI while using the service token for your CI/CD pipelines.</li>
<li class="">The new global <code>--token &lt;token></code> flag allows you to pass the service token used by requests requiring authentication. For example, to install an app, use: <code>slack install --token &lt;your-service-token></code>. To create a trigger, use: <code>slack trigger create --token &lt;your-service-token> --app deployed --trigger-def triggers/trigger_def_file.ts</code>. To deploy an app, use: <code>slack deploy --token &lt;your-service-token></code></li>
<li class="">We added support for a global <code>--experiment [name,name,...]</code> flag.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023/05/16/apis>The team.accessLogs method now supports cursor-based pagination</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-05-16T00:00:00.000Z>May 16, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Read more <a class="" href=/reference/methods/team.accessLogs#pagination>here</a>.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/new-feature>New Feature</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023/05/04/slack-cli>Release: Slack CLI v2.2.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-05-04T00:00:00.000Z>May 4, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Version <code>2.2.0</code> of the developer tools for our beta Slack platform has landed!</p>
<ul>
<li class="">The <code>trigger info</code> command now also shows who has permissions to run the trigger.</li>
<li class="">We added the <code>--no-color</code> flag, which removes all ANSI sequences for color as well as emojis, giving you plain text output from the CLI that's perfect for piping to a text file.</li>
<li class="">The <code>datastore query</code> command now supports a <code>cursor</code> argument to help you paginate your results the way you want.</li>
<li class="">Trigger operations will now let you know when an invalid trigger file is being ignored.</li>
<li class="">We improved error reporting and some help text.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023/05/02/apis>Message attachment field changes</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-05-02T00:00:00.000Z>May 2, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We're modifying text presented in Slack message attachments (links to other messages in Slack) via the <code>footer</code> and <code>channel_name</code> fields for consistency.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023/04/24/slack-cli>Introducing the Slack automations platform</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-04-24T00:00:00.000Z>April 24, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Today we're announcing that the <a class="" href=/workflows>Slack automations platform</a>—which provides a faster, more flexible way to build automations on top of Slack–is generally available to developers. The platform's overhauled architecture gives developers more ways to build, code, and ship custom apps and workflows more quickly and easily in an environment that's both secure and compliant. <a href=https://slack.com/blog/developers/next-gen-platform-launch target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Read the announcement</a> or follow the <a class="" href=/tools/deno-slack-sdk/guides/getting-started>Quickstart</a> to get started today.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023/04/20/preview>Beta release: Slack CLI v2.1.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-04-20T00:00:00.000Z>April 20, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We released version <code>v2.1.0</code> of the developer tools for our Slack platform beta. Changes include better error messages, including the local Git version with the <code>slack doctor</code> command, paring down which commands are visible with <code>slack help</code> to only what is applicable for developers, and more.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/beta>Beta</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023/03/23/preview>Beta release: Slack CLI v1.21.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-03-23T00:00:00.000Z>March 23, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We released version <code>v1.21.0</code> of the developer tools for our Slack platform beta. Changes include improved ergonomics around trigger access management and added a new command to export form responses to CSV, both within the CLI, updates to the default manifest, and more.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/beta>Beta</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023/02/23/preview>Beta release: Slack CLI v1.20.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-02-23T00:00:00.000Z>February 23, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We released <code>v1.20.0</code> of the developer tools for our Slack platform beta. Changes include a number of user-requested improvements to the CLI and details about an upcoming maintenance window next month, and breaking changes landing the month after that, which may require you to update your apps.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/beta>Beta</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023/02/09/preview>Beta release: Slack CLI v1.19.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-02-09T00:00:00.000Z>February 9, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We released version <code>v1.19.0</code> of the developer tools for our Slack platform beta.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/beta>Beta</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2023/02/01/preview>Beta release: Slack CLI v1.18.0</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2023-02-01T09:00:00.000Z>February 1, 2023</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We released version <code>v1.18.0</code> of the developer tools for our Slack platform beta. View our new <a href=https://github.com/slack-samples target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">curated collection of sample apps</a> for inspiration and illustration.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/release>Release</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/slack-cli>Slack CLI</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/beta>Beta</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2022/12/31/output>2022 changelog entries</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2022-12-31T00:00:00.000Z>December 31, 2022</time></div></header><div class=markdown><h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=november>November<a href=#november class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to November" title="Direct link to November" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">We released version <code>v1.16.4</code> of the developer tools for our Slack platform beta. We fixed some pipes behind the scenes to prevent future leaks; check out how we are improving the beta platform experience for our community.</li>
<li class="">Three new endpoints for admins to manage role assignments are now available: <code>admin.roles.listAssignments</code>, <code>admin.roles.addAssignments</code>, and <code>admin.roles.removeAssignments</code>. Explore other useful methods for managing your users and workspaces here.</li>
<li class="">We released version <code>v1.15.0</code> of the developer tools for our Slack platform beta. It also introduces a breaking change (arriving <strong>January 26th, 2023</strong>) for those making API calls to outgoing domains in their functions.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=october>October<a href=#october class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to October" title="Direct link to October" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">A bevy of new Block Kit input elements await developers soliciting input from users including the often requested combined date and time picker. Collect links with the URL input element or email addresses, numbers, too.</li>
<li class="">We released version <code>v1.14.0</code> of the developer tools for our Slack platform beta.</li>
<li class="">We updated the fine print and added default <code>placeholder</code> text for the following Block Kit elements: <code>channels_select</code>, <code>conversations_select</code>, <code>multi_channels_select</code>, <code>multi_users_select</code>, and <code>users_select</code>.</li>
<li class="">At last, member_joined_channel now works as you'd expect for multi-party direct messages (MPIM). Be sure to add the mpim<!-- -->:read<!-- --> scope to receive these events!</li>
<li class="">We're cleaning up some lingering behavior in our legacy Real Time Messaging API. In message events streamed over the RTM API, channel and usergroup mentions will no longer include entity names. Still need entity names? Access them using Web API methods such as <code>conversation.info</code> and <code>usergroups.list</code>. Alternatively, consider using the Events API, which also supports WebSockets, to receive <code>message</code> events.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=september>September<a href=#september class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to September" title="Direct link to September" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Today we permanently alter the behavior of the retired Web API method <code>rtm.start</code>: those still using this method will receive the more reliable but brief response of the <code>rtm.connect</code> method.</li>
<li class="">To better accommodate customers at Dreamforce next week, we've moved <code>rtm.start</code>'s final retirement date to <strong>September 27th, 2022</strong>. Learn more about the future of <code>rtm.start</code> and how it may impact your app.</li>
<li class="">Several new tools for app developers are now available as part of our Slack platform open beta. Developers can ship higher-quality apps and workflows quickly with a streamlined development lifecycle, including secure hosting and data storage in Slack.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=august>August<a href=#august class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to August" title="Direct link to August" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Keep track of who gets added to DM conversations. You can now monitor the <code>dm_user_added</code> audit event with the Audit Logs API.</li>
<li class="">On <strong>September 13th, 2022</strong>, we will provide a preview of the <code>rtm.start</code> future behavior. If you still use <code>rtm.start</code> to connect to Slack, learn more about when this preview will be happening in your time zone and how it may impact your app.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=july>July<a href=#july class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to July" title="Direct link to July" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Slack is used by public sector teams and their partners for being faster, better organized, and more secure than email. If you're a government agency, contractor, or just intrigued by how Slack supports government communication, our GovSlack documentation is the place to be!</li>
<li class="">Bring users information and delight in your Slack apps with the video block now available in Block Kit. Read on to learn more on how to embed videos in your app.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=may>May<a href=#may class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to May" title="Direct link to May" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Be informed about specific changes to users' data. One of three events will now be dispatched alongside the <code>user_change</code> event: <code>user_huddle_changed</code>, <code>user_profile_changed</code>, or <code>user_status_changed</code>.</li>
<li class="">The file may be deleted, but the record of the event won't be. You can now monitor <code>file_deleted</code> audit events with the Audit Logs API.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=april>April<a href=#april class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to April" title="Direct link to April" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Messages are how people communicate in Slack, message metadata is how apps communicate with apps! Read on to learn about how to spark more automation with your app throughout Slack.</li>
<li class="">The <code>team.info</code> parameter <code>domain</code> is now public. Query for your team's information by <code>domain</code> only when <code>team</code> is null.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=march>March<a href=#march class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to March" title="Direct link to March" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Mentioning a private channel in a slash command when your app manifest flag <code>should_escape</code> is <code>false</code> now correctly formats the channel identifier. Previously, the API would return HTML entities (<code>&amp;lt;</code> and <code>&amp;gt;</code>) that had to be manually converted into their character counterparts.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=february>February<a href=#february class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to February" title="Direct link to February" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Help users find links, messages, and files germane to a channel's distinctive purpose with the Bookmarks API.</li>
<li class="">The <code>admin.users.unsupportedVersions.export</code> API allows you to export users using unsupported software within your workspace. Read on to learn more.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=january>January<a href=#january class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to January" title="Direct link to January" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Block Kit button elements can now utilize the optional <code>accessibility_label</code> field, which allows you to write longer descriptive text for a button. Learn more.</li>
<li class="">The <code>admin.apps.requests.cancel</code> method allows admins to cancel app approval requests within a workspace or Enterprise org. Learn more.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/compilation>Compilation</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2021/12/31/>2021 shortform changelog entries</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2021-12-31T00:00:00.000Z>December 31, 2021</time></div></header><div class=markdown><h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=november>November<a href=#november class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to November" title="Direct link to November" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">If you still use <code>rtm.connect</code> or <code>rtm.start</code> to connect to Slack, you'll notice that all WebSocket URLs now begin with <code>wss://wss-primary.slack.com</code>.</li>
<li class="">As previously announced, apps & integrations created after today, <strong>November 30, 2021</strong>, must use <code>rtm.connect</code> instead of the deprecated <code>rtm.start</code> when connecting to the RTM API.</li>
<li class="">Block elements can now utilize the <code>focus_on_load</code> field within Block kit messages, which allows you to pick one specific Block element to auto focus on.</li>
<li class="">The default Slack Connect invitation type when using <code>conversations.inviteShared</code> has changed. Invites are now sent to limit the recipient's actions to only sending messages. The new <code>external_limited</code> argument can be used to control which invitation type is sent.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=october>October<a href=#october class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to October" title="Direct link to October" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">We're starting to roll out a new, opt-in beta UI that lets you configure and reconfigure apps using manifests. We're also launching new App Manifest APIs to let you create and manage all your apps programmatically.</li>
<li class="">One of our earliest API methods is taking a well-deserved retirement on <strong>September 27, 2022</strong>. For existing apps, <code>rtm.start</code> will instead return an equivalent response to <code>rtm.connect</code>. Beginning <strong>November 30, 2021</strong>, <em>newly</em> created apps and integrations will only be able to use <code>rtm.connect</code>.</li>
<li class="">Introducing two API methods that return information about workspaces previously only available in <code>rtm.start</code>: <code>team.billing.info</code> and <code>team.preferences.list</code>.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=september>September<a href=#september class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to September" title="Direct link to September" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class=""><a href=https://sdt.builtbyslack.com target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Slack Developer Tools</a> now offers the <em>Platform Guide</em>, an interactive and introductory education experience for developers interested in learning the basics of building a Slack app <em>within</em> a Slack app.</li>
<li class="">Pick a time, any time. The <code>timepicker</code> block element is released out of <code>beta</code> and available to use in your spiffy apps.</li>
<li class="">The <code>link_shared</code> event is changing, bringing unfurls—allowing users to see what's in a link—into the message composer.</li>
<li class="">In the app approval APIs, you may now distinguish the apps built within your organization from those developed externally—or by Slack—with the <code>developer_type</code> field.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=august>August<a href=#august class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to August" title="Direct link to August" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Legacy workspace apps are now completely retired. They won't function anymore and eventually will be completely removed from our databases. If you run into trouble, <a href=https://my.slack.com/help/requests/new target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">please reach out</a>.</li>
<li class="">The <code>link_shared</code> event is changing to bring a little more magic to app unfurls. Read up on the changes, which roll out to free teams on <strong>September 1, 2021</strong>.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=july>July<a href=#july class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to July" title="Direct link to July" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Modern Sign in with Slack uses the <a href=https://openid.net/specs/openid-connect-core-1_0.html target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">OpenID Connect</a> protocol to make signing in with Slack faster and more flexible. Try it today.</li>
<li class="">Refresh your access tokens regularly with token rotation, available for opt-in now.</li>
<li class="">You can now manage Slack Connect directly for your organization using an app. Read up on the Slack Connect APIs.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=june>June<a href=#june class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to June" title="Direct link to June" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">We gave this dusty place a new coat of paint. Enjoy our updates to api.slack.com to help you navigate, discover, and absorb content more easily. Almost everything should be where you’d expect it.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=may>May<a href=#may class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to May" title="Direct link to May" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Use manifests to create and manage apps from saveable, shareable, and relatable YAML and JSON. Try out some sample manifests in our new guided tutorials.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=april>April<a href=#april class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to April" title="Direct link to April" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Apps using classic message attachments have an updated look. Attachment images now have a hover menu and will mostly appear to the right of text. Consider using Block Kit to have more control over how images render.</li>
<li class="">We're teaching old blocks new tricks. Starting <strong>April 20, 2021</strong> <code>input</code> blocks are now able to exist within messages, allowing you to gather information more swiftly within conversation.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=march>March<a href=#march class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to March" title="Direct link to March" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Apps may now broadcast messages to users via direct message without handling unnecessary or unsupported conversation and slash commands. Starting <strong>March 29, 2021</strong>, this feature will be <em>default</em> for all <em>newly-created</em> Slack apps. Get started by visiting the App Home tab of your existing Slack apps.</li>
<li class="">Newly created private channel IDs now always begin with the letter <code>C</code>, just like public channel IDs already do. The Conversations API will tell you whether a conversation is private or not with the <code>is_private</code> boolean field.</li>
<li class="">Legacy workspace apps, deprecated since October 2018, will officially retire on <strong>August 24, 2021</strong>.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=february>February<a href=#february class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to February" title="Direct link to February" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">The <code>admin.analytics.getFile</code> method now returns daily data about conversations in public channels. Members analytics remain available. Explore what's happening on your Enterprise org workspaces.</li>
<li class="">Three deprecations take effect today, <strong>February 24,2021</strong>. First, new apps may no longer pass tokens as query parameters. Second, Conversations API methods are now required over their typed counterparts: <code>channel.*</code>, <code>group.*</code>, <code>im.*</code>, and <code>mpim.*</code>. Third, event payloads no longer contain full lists of <code>authed_users</code> or <code>authed_teams</code>—instead, use a new method to learn the full list of authorizations an event is visible to. We know keeping up with best practices for Slack apps is a lot to handle—thank you for allowing us to make the platform better. Keep reading.</li>
<li class="">If your app makes use of user emails, be on the lookout for <em>relay email addresses</em>. When users sign into Slack via Apple, their emails may appear as anonymized relay addresses. Relatedly, Sign in with Slack won't work with these users.</li>
<li class="">Now you can decorate your ephemeral messages requesting authorization with Block Kit using <code>chat.unfurl</code>.</li>
<li class="">When a user initiates a private channel share via Slack Connect, the channel's ID <em>changes</em>. Subscribe to <code>channel_id_changed</code> to learn the new IDs for the private channels visible to your app.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=january>January<a href=#january class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to January" title="Direct link to January" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Updated: Beginning mid-March, links appearing in Block Kit messages shared by apps will unfurl just like other links found in that message.</li>
<li class="">Your app can now count its workflow steps with the help of four new events: <code>workflow_published</code>, <code>workflow_unpublished</code>, <code>workflow_deleted</code>, and <code>workflow_step_deleted</code>. Use these events to stay informed on workflows—from unpublished to published and back again—that make use of steps powered by your app.</li>
<li class="">Socket Mode supplies your app with events and interactive feature payloads over a dynamic WebSocket URL.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/compilation>Compilation</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2021-10-changes-to-admin-app-requests>Changes to admin apps requests</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2021-10-30T00:00:00.000Z>October 30, 2021</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p><code>admin.apps.requests.list</code> API is enhanced to fetch Org AAA requests using <strong>enterprise_id</strong> arg.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/new-feature>New feature</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Changes to admin apps requests" href=/changelog/2021-10-changes-to-admin-app-requests><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2021-10-manifest-a-new-reality>Rolling out a new beta app settings experience</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2021-10-30T00:00:00.000Z>October 30, 2021</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Starting on <strong>October 7, 2021</strong>, we will start rolling out a new beta app settings experience. This new UI will allow you to directly edit an app's manifest to update its configuration.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/beta>Beta</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Rolling out a new beta app settings experience" href=/changelog/2021-10-manifest-a-new-reality><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2021-10-rtm-start-to-stop>rtm.start to stop</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2021-10-05T09:00:00.000Z>October 5, 2021</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>The original way to connect to one of our oldest APIs is finally retiring. For existing apps, <a class="" href=/reference/methods/rtm.start><code>rtm.start</code></a> will start behaving exactly like <a class="" href=/reference/methods/rtm.connect><code>rtm.connect</code></a> on <strong>September 27, 2022</strong>. Beginning November 30, 2021, newly created apps and integrations will only be able to use <code>rtm.connect</code>.</p>
<p>The RTM API remains available to developers using <code>rtm.connect</code>.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/deprecation>Deprecation</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>Breaking change</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about rtm.start to stop" href=/changelog/2021-10-rtm-start-to-stop><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2021-08-changes-to-unfurls>Changes to unfurls</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2021-08-30T09:00:00.000Z>August 30, 2021</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>On September 1, 2021, the <a class="" href=/reference/events/link_shared><code>link_shared</code></a> event is changing. The change will happen for free teams on September 1, and will roll out to paid teams over the following weeks.</p>
<p>The <a class="" href=/reference/methods/chat.unfurl><code>chat.unfurl</code></a> method will also accept new arguments.</p>
<p>Changes to <code>link_shared</code> will help enable a smoother unfurl experience for apps that haven't yet been installed.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div><div datetime=2021-08-30T00:00:00.000Z>August 30, 2021</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p><code>admin.apps.requests.list</code> API response is enhanced to include the <strong>is_user_app_collaborator</strong> of the app.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/new-feature>New feature</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Changes to 2021</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Admin apps API response is enhanced to include the <strong>developer_type</strong> of the app.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/new-feature>New feature</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Changes to admin apps" href=/changelog/2021-08-changes-to-admin-apps><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2021-02-how-we-broke-your-slack-app>How we broke your Slack app</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2021-02-24T00:00:00.000Z>February 24, 2021</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Hello! You are here because three monumental things changed on the Slack platform today, February 24, 2021.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/deprecation>Deprecation</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>Breaking change</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about How we broke your Slack app" href=/changelog/2021-02-how-we-broke-your-slack-app><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2021-01-workspace-apps-retiring-the-platform-graveyard-in-aug-2021>Goodbye, workspace apps</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2021-01-30T00:00:00.000Z>January 30, 2021</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>On <strong>August 24, 2021, legacy workspace apps</strong> were retired. Workspace apps were part of a brief developer preview we elected to not fully release. Since October 2018, existing workspace apps have remained functional but on August 24, 2021 workspace apps will be retired and no longer function.</p>
<p>Please read on if you were the developer, maintainer, administrator, or user of a vintage workspace app.</p>
<p>Don't know if you have a workspace app? Make sure you're signed in to all your workspaces and visit our <a href=https://api.slack.com/apps target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class=""><strong>deprecation center</strong></a>. Each workspace app you own or collaborate on will be listed.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/deprecation>Deprecation</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>Breaking change</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Goodbye, workspace apps" href=/changelog/2021-01-workspace-apps-retiring-the-platform-graveyard-in-aug-2021><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2020/12/31/compilation>2020 shortform changelog entries</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2020-12-31T00:00:00.000Z>December 31, 2020</time></div></header><div class=markdown><h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=december>December<a href=#december class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to December" title="Direct link to December" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Submissions to the Slack Marketplace now require Security & Compliance information.</li>
<li class="">Reach a whole new world of workspaces: build an app that can be deployed across an entire Enterprise org.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=november>November<a href=#november class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to November" title="Direct link to November" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Apps created after <strong>February 24, 2021</strong> will no longer be able to send <code>token</code> as a query parameter. All existing apps require no changes.</li>
<li class="">Apps will now be able to unfurl links anywhere in Slack.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=october>October<a href=#october class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to October" title="Direct link to October" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">The admin.analytics.getFile method returns compressed JSON files with workspace member analytics for the day of your choice—now available for Enterprise.</li>
<li class="">App <a class="" href=/surfaces/modals>modals</a> can now be 'popped out' by users, giving them their own resizable, movable window. No app changes are needed, we just wanted to pop in with an update.</li>
<li class="">To simplify time input for users, we added a new time picker element to Block Kit.</li>
<li class="">Block Kit checkboxes and radio buttons are now available to use in messages. Quickly and conversationally collect information from users by including them inline.</li>
<li class="">Gather data from users directly from your App Home—input blocks can now be added to Home tabs. Additionally, input blocks can now dispatch <code>block_actions</code> payloads when someone interacts with them. Read about the new <code>dispatch_actions</code> flag.</li>
<li class="">We refreshed the look of your app's listing in the Slack Marketplace. Among the changes: a <em>Features</em> tab shows your app's entry points—like shortcuts and slash commands.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=september>September<a href=#september class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to September" title="Direct link to September" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">We updated our <a href=https://slack.com/terms-of-service/api-updated target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">developer policy and API terms of service</a> to clarify language around export controls and international data transfers.</li>
<li class="">Alongside upcoming changes to the Events API, you'll find numerous new features: a new <code>authorizations</code> field delivered with events, a new method for listing installations, a new scope—even a new token type for working across an entire organization.</li>
<li class="">Starting <strong>February 24, 2021</strong>, event payloads will no longer contain full lists of <code>authed_users</code> or <code>authed_teams</code>. Instead, you can call a separate method if you need a full list of parties an event is visible to.</li>
<li class="">On <strong>September 29, 2020</strong>, <code>view_submission</code> and <code>block_actions</code> payloads will begin including full <code>state</code> for messages, modal, and App Home views.</li>
<li class="">On <strong>September 15, 2020</strong>, you'll no longer need to worry about different <em>global</em> and <em>local</em> IDs for Enterprise users. Users will have a single, global ID across an Enterprise org, which may begin with <em>either</em> <code>U</code> or <code>W</code>.</li>
<li class="">In responses from the <code>search.messages</code> method, four fields—<code>next</code>, <code>next_2</code>, <code>previous</code>, and <code>previous_2</code>—that sometimes appeared are now deprecated and will no longer appear in responses, beginning <strong>December 3, 2020</strong>.</li>
<li class="">Get a handle on creating channels, setting preferences, and connecting new workspaces—all with a single app. Use the APIs for channel management, available to Enterprise organizations.</li>
<li class="">We <em>slightly</em> changed your App Home's appearance by refreshing the default text style and how hint text is displayed. We hope you'll enjoy it.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=august>August<a href=#august class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to August" title="Direct link to August" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Users may now mute and unmute their conversations with apps <a href=https://slack.com/help/articles/204411433-Mute-channels-and-direct-messages target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">like they can with other channel types</a>. When a user mutes a conversation with your app, the messages you send are still delivered and a colorful badge will continue to surface in their channel list. However, users will not receive a direct operating system or browser notification on delivery.</li>
<li class="">Slash command invocations will now include an <code>api_app_id</code> parameter with your Slack app's ID. This parameter will better assist you in handling commands from multiple applications or environments.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=july>July<a href=#july class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to July" title="Direct link to July" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">New header blocks let you provide stronger delineation between groups of content in your app surfaces. Stay a<em>head</em> of the game by learning how they work.</li>
<li class="">Expand Workflow Builder's capabilities by creating reusable, custom steps that any builder can add to their workflows. Workflow Steps from Apps is now in open beta. What’s your app’s next step?</li>
<li class="">Previously, when a user mentioned an app that wasn't party to the conversation, the user could <code>Invite</code> the app to the conversation, <code>Let Them Know</code>, or <code>Do Nothing</code>. The <code>Let Them Know</code> button didn't work. We've fixed that mistake by removing the button, and updated our documentation on the <code>app_mention</code> event as well.</li>
<li class="">Mark messages unread for users with <code>conversations.mark</code>. Bespoke clients and personal utilities should use this method sparingly.</li>
<li class="">The URL where users manage existing installations of Slack apps is changing to <a href=https://app.slack.com/apps-manage/ target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class=""><code>https://app.slack.com/apps-manage/</code></a>. You might not even notice the difference, but we’re letting you know just in case.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=june>June<a href=#june class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to June" title="Direct link to June" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">You can now present your app's pricing information in your listing in the Slack Marketplace.</li>
<li class="">With Slack Connect, channels connect multiple workspaces and organizations with ease.</li>
<li class="">A change to <code>user_change</code> events: we've fixed a bug where these events dispatched to subscriptions from all workspaces in externally-shared channels. Now, <code>user_change</code> events are dispatched only to the home workspace of an externally-shared channel.</li>
<li class="">If you create a <em>new</em> Slack app and use deprecated methods like <code>channels.*</code>, <code>im.*</code>, <code>mpim.*</code>, or <code>groups.*</code>, you'll now receive a <code>method_deprecated</code> error.  <em>Existing</em> apps will receive <em>warnings</em> but still have until <strong>February 24th, 2021</strong> to migrate to the Conversations API.</li>
<li class="">Maintain a membership allowlist for private channels using <code>admin.conversations.restrictAccess.addGroup</code>, <code>admin.conversations.restrictAccess.removeGroup</code>, & <code>admin.conversations.restrictAccess.listGroups</code> methods, now available for Enterprise organizations. <em>Update</em>: These methods were renamed but the old names will continue to work.</li>
<li class="">We recently updated <a href=https://app.slack.com/block-kit-builder target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Block Kit Builder</a> with additional preview options and more convenient ways to copy, paste, and dispatch payloads. There's more beauty to it too.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=may>May<a href=#may class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to May" title="Direct link to May" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">The deadline for all Slack apps to use the Conversations API—instead of its antecedents—has moved from this November to <strong>February 24th, 2021</strong>. Newly created Slack apps won't be able to use <code>channels.*</code>, <code>im.*</code>, <code>mpim.*</code>, or <code>groups.*</code> methods beginning <strong>June 10th, 2020</strong>. Warnings will soon be included as part of deprecated responses.</li>
<li class="">Use the Calls API to hook your calls natively into Slack. Catch up on Calls.</li>
<li class="">Legacy tester tokens may no longer be created. Existing tokens may continue to be used, regenerated, or revoked. Tokens left unused for three months or more will be regularly revoked.from our previous announcement.</li>
<li class=""><a href=https://slack.com/help/articles/115001435788-Connect-identity-provider-groups-to-your-Enterprise-organization target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Complete your IDP groups</a> with custom default channels, courtesy of the <code>admin.usergroups.*</code> API methods.</li>
<li class="">Starting <strong>July 1st, 2020</strong>, rate limits will apply to all SCIM methods. Please make sure any apps using the SCIM APIs remain within these limits and humbly handle HTTP 429 responses.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=april>April<a href=#april class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to April" title="Direct link to April" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">A more direct route to messaging in response to modals: the new <code>default_to_current_conversation</code> field allows your <code>conversation_select</code> and <code>multi_conversation_select</code> menus to be pre-populate the currently open conversation.</li>
<li class="">The shortcuts button is now available for all Slack workspaces, so we're taking global shortcuts out of beta.</li>
<li class="">Previously, OAuth Redirect URLs could contain anchors (<code>#</code>). We've fixed that mistake, and anchors are no longer allowed.</li>
<li class="">Beginning <strong>June 10th, 2020</strong>, all newly created Slack apps will be unable to use the deprecated methods in <code>channels.*</code>, <code>im.*</code>, <code>mpim.*</code>, and <code>groups.*</code>. Existing apps have until <strong>February 24th, 2021</strong> to migrate to the Conversations API.</li>
<li class="">Visually highlight destructive actions by using the new <code>style</code> parameter in confirmation objects.</li>
<li class="">Give app installers good reason to trust your app: submit security and compliance information to the Slack Marketplace today.</li>
<li class="">SCIM API endpoints now have clear, explicit rate limits.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=march>March<a href=#march class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to March" title="Direct link to March" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Tune out the noise—you can now use filters with conversation lists in select and multi-select menus.and start filtering.</li>
<li class="">Give users clear entry points to your Slack app with Shortcuts. App Actions are now called message shortcuts. They're joined by new global shortcuts that allow users to initiate interactivity from anywhere in Slack.</li>
<li class="">The IDs returned by our APIs have grown longer. They are now up to 11 characters long, and could grow longer in future. Please audit your Slack apps, and verify any assumptions about the length of IDs for users, channels, and other objects.</li>
<li class="">We didn't turn off the <code>replies</code> array field found in threaded parent messages on <strong>October 18th, 2019</strong> like we said we would. The new date is <strong>March 31st, 2020</strong>. Please use the <code>reply_users</code>, <code>reply_users_count</code>, and <code>latest_reply</code> fields instead.</li>
<li class="">Fair is fair: radio buttons now support <code>mrkdwn</code> formatting, just like checkboxes.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=february>February<a href=#february class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to February" title="Direct link to February" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">New guidelines for Slack Marketplace submissions have arrived to help ready your app for the world.</li>
<li class="">Using two new scopes, your Slack app can adjust its message authorship and post in any public channel.</li>
<li class="">The creation of legacy test tokens is now deprecated and will permanently retire on <strong>May 5th, 2020</strong>.about using Slack apps to build firmly scoped integrations.</li>
<li class="">Starting <strong>February 18, 2020</strong>, unexpected results using the SCIM API when rapidly updating data on the same user or group will become a thing of the past.</li>
<li class="">It's a win for webhooks: you can skip the small stuff and <a href=https://slack.com/help/articles/360041352714 target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">trigger a workflow with a web request</a>.</li>
<li class="">Check another item off your Block Kit wishlist - we've added a checkbox group element to modals and Home tabs for your multiple choice input needs.</li>
<li class="">You can submit information to the Slack Marketplace on your app's privacy policy, data retention, security tests, and compliance with major laws. <a href=https://medium.com/slack-developer-blog/building-trust-with-security-conscious-customers-1e85ee856045 target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Read our blog post on the new Security & Compliance feature, now in open beta</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=january>January<a href=#january class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to January" title="Direct link to January" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Our new emoji APIs allow Enterprise organization Admins and Owners to add, remove, list, rename, and alias custom emoji across the entire Enterprise organization. <!-- -->🎉<!-- -->!</li>
<li class="">Slack apps, with subtler permissions and more intuitive behavior, are now the default when you create an app. Get started by building or migrating.</li>
<li class="">Your app's new Home tab is out of beta. Design a comfortable place for users to get work done using Block Kit Builder and publish them for users using <code>views.publish</code>. Get started by diving into the Home tab docs.</li>
<li class="">Give users a key to directly open your Home tab. Read our updated deep-linking guide to see how you can create links to specific tabs in your App Home.</li>
<li class="">We are deprecating all <code>channels.*</code>, <code>groups.*</code>, <code>im.*</code>, and <code>mpim.*</code> Web API methods in favor of their Conversations API replacements. Migrate to <code>conversations.*</code> as soon as possible, as these deprecated methods will retire on <strong>February 24, 2021</strong>.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/compilation>Compilation</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2020/11/01/app-unfurls-everywhere>App unfurls everywhere</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2020-11-01T00:00:00.000Z>November 1, 2020</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Until now, it's often been confusing to understand when and where an app may provide customized unfurl behavior for links appearing in conversations. We're gradually rolling out changes that will make this behavior consistent and easily understood. Read on to learn more.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about App unfurls everywhere" href=/changelog/2020/11/01/app-unfurls-everywhere><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2020-11-no-more-tokens-in-querystrings-for-newly-created-apps>No more tokens in querystrings for newly created apps</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2020-11-01T00:00:00.000Z>November 1, 2020</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Tokens may no longer be passed in the query string for apps created after Feb 24, 2021</p>
<p>On <strong>February 24, 2021</strong>, we will stop allowing <em>newly created</em> Slack apps to send requests to <a class="" href=/reference/methods>Web API methods</a> with access tokens presented in a URL query string. Instead, apps must send tokens in the <code>Authorization</code> HTTP header or alternatively as a URL-encoded POST body parameter.</p>
<p>Existing apps will be allowed to continue sending their tokens in the <code>token</code> query string parameter, though we recommend all apps to use authorization headers whenever possible.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about No more tokens in querystrings for newly created apps" href=/changelog/2020-11-no-more-tokens-in-querystrings-for-newly-created-apps><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2020-09-15-events-api-truncate-authed-users>Events API truncate authed users</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2020-09-15T00:00:00.000Z>September 15, 2020</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Your app's <a class="" href=/reference/events>events</a>—received from the <a class="" href=/apis/events-api/>Events API</a>—are changing.</p>
<p>Event payloads will no longer contain a full list of <code>authed_users</code> or <code>authed_teams</code>. These two fields will be deprecated. There'll be a new, compact field called <code>authorizations</code> to replace them—<strong>but</strong> <code>authorizations</code> will only contain <em>at most one</em> person or workspace that the event is visible to.</p>
<p>If you need a <em>full</em> list of all the parties an event is visible to, you'll <a href=#what class="">call the <code>apps.event.authorizations.list</code> method</a>.</p>
<p>The new, streamlined shape of events allows Slack to deliver them faster.</p>
<p>These changes to the Events API will take place on <strong>February 24, 2021</strong>. You'll be able to <strong>opt in</strong> to them earlier, on September 29, 2020, by going to your <a href=https://api.slack.com/apps target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">app settings</a> and selecting the checkbox under <strong>Event Subscription</strong>.</p>
<p>In order to get ready for the changes to authorizations, you can use the <a href=#what class=""><code>apps.event.authorizations.list</code></a> method <strong>even without opting in</strong> to the new shape of events, starting September 29, 2020.</p>
<p>Read on for more details on <a href=#what class="">what's changing</a> and <a href=#how class="">how to prepare</a>.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/deprecation>Deprecation</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>Breaking change</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Events API truncate authed users" href=/changelog/2020-09-15-events-api-truncate-authed-users><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2020/09/01/full-state-on-view-submisson-and-block-actions>A full state on view submission and block actions</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2020-09-01T00:00:00.000Z>September 1, 2020</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>If you rely or want to rely on stateful Block Kit views, we have some exciting news for you. The payloads for <a class="" href=/reference/interaction-payloads/view-interactions-payload#view_submission><code>view_submission</code></a> and <a class="" href=/reference/interaction-payloads/block_actions-payload><code>block_actions</code></a> will have some new additions. Read on to learn more.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/new-feature>New feature</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about A full state on view submission and block actions" href=/changelog/2020/09/01/full-state-on-view-submisson-and-block-actions><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2020/09/01/minor-developer-policy-update>Minor developer policy update</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2020-09-01T00:00:00.000Z>September 1, 2020</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>On September 30, 2020 we updated the <a class="" href=/developer-policy>Slack Application Developer Policy</a> and <a href=https://slack.com/terms-of-service/api-updated target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">API Terms of Service</a> to clarify existing guidelines.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Minor developer policy update" href=/changelog/2020/09/01/minor-developer-policy-update><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2020-02-legacy-test-token-creation-to-retire>Legacy test token creation to retire</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2020-02-01T00:00:00.000Z>February 1, 2020</time></div></header><div class=markdown><div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-warning admonition_xJq3 alert alert--warning"><div class=admonitionHeading_Gvgb><span class=admonitionIcon_Rf37><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill-rule=evenodd d="M8.893 1.5c-.183-.31-.52-.5-.887-.5s-.703.19-.886.5L.138 13.499a.98.98 0 0 0 0 1.001c.193.31.53.501.886.501h13.964c.367 0 .704-.19.877-.5a1.03 1.03 0 0 0 .01-1.002L8.893 1.5zm.133 11.497H6.987v-2.003h2.039v2.003zm0-3.004H6.987V5.987h2.039v4.006z"/></svg></span>Legacy tester tokens may no longer be created.</div></div>
<p>We're deprecating <a class="" href=/legacy/legacy-custom-integrations/legacy-custom-integrations-tokens>legacy test tokens</a> and will disallow the creation of new test tokens beginning <strong>May 5th, 2020</strong>.</p>
<p>We launched Slack apps over four years ago as a replacement to the number of ways one could obtain overly-permissive tokens to integrate with Slack.</p>
<p>If you or a software product you author relies on test token creation, you will need to migrate to using Slack apps with specifically named scopes instead.</p>
<p>Existing tester tokens will continue functioning but tokens left unused are subject to periodic revocation.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/deprecation>Deprecation</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>Breaking change</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Legacy test token creation to retire" href=/changelog/2020-02-legacy-test-token-creation-to-retire><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2020-01-deprecating-antecedents-to-the-conversations-api>Deprecating antecedents to the conversations API</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2020-01-07T00:00:00.000Z>January 7, 2020</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We released the <a class="" href=/apis/web-api/using-the-conversations-api>Conversations API</a> in September 2017 as a one-size-fits-all replacement for a variety of APIs used to read and write information about channels, private channels, direct messages, and multi-party direct messages.</p>
<p>Today we are announcing the deprecation of the methods that preceded the Conversations API (<code>channels.*</code>, <code>groups.*</code>, <code>im.*</code>, & <code>mpim.*</code>). On <strike>November 25th, 2020</strike> <strong>February 24th, 2021</strong> these methods will retire and cease functioning.</p>
<p>If users expect your app to work in channels of any kind, you'll want to verify you're using the Conversations API for all channel types.</p>
