<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-warning admonition_xJq3 alert alert--warning"><div class=admonitionHeading_Gvgb><span class=admonitionIcon_Rf37><svg viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill-rule=evenodd d="M8.893 1.5c-.183-.31-.52-.5-.887-.5s-.703.19-.886.5L.138 13.499a.98.98 0 0 0 0 1.001c.193.31.53.501.886.501h13.964c.367 0 .704-.19.877-.5a1.03 1.03 0 0 0 .01-1.002L8.893 1.5zm.133 11.497H6.987v-2.003h2.039v2.003zm0-3.004H6.987V5.987h2.039v4.006z"/></svg></span>The final date for existing apps and custom integrations is now February 24th, 2021</div><div class=admonitionContent_BuS1><p>We'll stop allowing <em>newly created</em> Slack apps to use these deprecated APIs beginning June 10th, 2020.<p>All <code>channels.*</code>, <code>groups.*</code>, <code>im.*</code>, & <code>mpim.*</code> methods will return <a href=#warnings class="">deprecation warnings</a> beginning June 10th, 2020.</div></div>
<p><strong>We resolutely recommend migrating to the Conversations API immediately.</strong></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/deprecation>Deprecation</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>Breaking change</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Deprecating antecedents to the conversations API" href=/changelog/2020-01-deprecating-antecedents-to-the-conversations-api><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2019/12/31/compilation>2019 shortform changelog entries</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2019-12-31T00:00:00.000Z>December 31, 2019</time></div></header><div class=markdown><h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=december>December<a href=#december class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to December" title="Direct link to December" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">We didn't set out to produce almost 700 pages of documentation but you can search it all now on api.slack.com/search.</li>
<li class="">Slack apps may now be submitted to the Slack Marketplace.</li>
<li class="">Place useful limits on multi-select menus using the new <code>max_selected_items</code> parameter.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=november>November<a href=#november class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to November" title="Direct link to November" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Your App home is going mobile — you can now interact with an app's Home tab from iOS and Android clients. We recently published a new App home tutorial to help you build, or you can read the Home tab docs.</li>
<li class="">Help users make informed decisions when considering your app by listing the languages it's fluent in and any pricing model that applies to it. You can provide this info as part of the Slack Marketplace submission process.</li>
<li class="">You can now use Block Kit radio buttons in modals, in addition to Home tabs.</li>
<li class="">We're removing the misleading and undocumented <code>guest_channels</code> field from user profile objects belonging to guest users. The <code>users.conversations</code> method is an accurate way to query the channels a guest user belongs to.</li>
<li class="">Slack has but one REST API, the SCIM API, and it's now fully standards-compliant with SCIM 1.1 when using the HTTP PATCH method to update user records.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=october>October<a href=#october class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to October" title="Direct link to October" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Your apps have always needed a better home, right in Slack. Now apps with bot users can use Block Kit with a new surface called the <em>Home tab</em>. Learn how to use this new space to provide users with a persistent place for dynamic experiences.</li>
<li class="">Radio is alive and well in Block Kit. Obtain a singular choice from users using our new radio button elements.</li>
<li class="">Craft a workspace faster than a cup of coffee and fill it with users, admins, and owners. Check out the APIs for creating workspaces and managing users, now available for Enterprise organizations.</li>
<li class="">Slack apps can act independently of a user token. Build a bot user powered by only the specific permissions it needs. Check out our open beta for newly created Slack apps.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=september>September<a href=#september class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to September" title="Direct link to September" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Announcing new pastures for Block Kit beyond messaging: trigger dynamic modal interfaces to provide linked user experiences invoked from messages, actions, or slash commands.</li>
<li class="">Embrace procrastination — allow users choose from multiple options in interactive workflows. Use new multi-select menus in all your Block Kit surfaces.</li>
<li class="">This autumn or soon thereafter, users will begin editing messages using a WYSIWYG (<em>what you see is what you get</em>) interface. When they do, their posted messages will appear slightly different throughout our APIs.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=august>August<a href=#august class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to August" title="Direct link to August" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Two new events, <code>channel_shared</code> and <code>channel_unshared</code>, now notify your app when a channel is shared or unshared.</li>
<li class="">A single admin app can now approve or restrict other app installs across an entire Enterprise org. Get a little meta, and a lot more time-efficient, with the APIs for app management.</li>
<li class="">As previously announced, <code>pins.add</code> will stop accepting file and file comment IDs beginning <strong>August 22, 2019</strong>. Similarly, <code>reactions.add</code> will no longer allow file and file comment parameters. Nowadays, apps and users pin & react to messages <em>about</em> files instead.</li>
<li class="">On <strong>March 4, 2020</strong>, we'll require all apps, custom integrations, bots, and users communicating with Slack to use TLS version <code>1.2</code> or higher. There will be a 24 hour test deprecation on <strong>February 19th, 2020</strong>. Read more details on why and how to upgrade.</li>
<li class="">Channel names have grown up: instead of a maximum length of 21 characters, channel names may now feature a full 80 character label.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=july>July<a href=#july class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to July" title="Direct link to July" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Host files wherever you please, while you add, update, remove, share, and unfurl them in Slack. Read up on the new Remote Files API.</li>
<li class="">Enterprise org admins may now use the <code>admin.users.session.reset</code> method to wipe a user session, logging out a user whose device may have been stolen or compromised.about the new method, as well as the new scope required to use it.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=june>June<a href=#june class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to June" title="Direct link to June" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Your app may now encounter channels shared between workspaces in an Enterprise org. As a result, it's even more important to use the Conversations API methods to safely handle channels both shared and unshared.</li>
<li class="">Using the SCIM API's <code>GET /Users</code> or <code>/Groups</code> methods? Their <code>count</code> parameters will no longer accept values above <code>1000</code> beginning <strong>August 30, 2019</strong>.</li>
<li class="">As announced previously, the <code>dnd.teamInfo</code> method now <em>requires</em> the <code>users</code> parameter. An explicit list of <code>users</code> helps you, and us, avoid slow API calls.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=may>May<a href=#may class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to May" title="Direct link to May" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">As previously announced, the <code>files.comments.add</code> and <code>files.comments.edit</code> methods are retiring today. Also, files may no longer be pinned to channels. The <code>pins.add</code> method will no longer accept files or file comments beginning <strong>August 22, 2019</strong>.</li>
<li class="">Better built-ins. Nifty type hints. Easier RTM event handling. Build for the future with the <a href=https://github.com/slackapi/python-slackclient target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">new Python Slack SDK V2.0.0</a>, lovingly crafted with Python 3.</li>
<li class="">Want to build a Slack app with JavaScript? Use the <a href=https://github.com/slackapi/bolt target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Bolt</a> framework. Effortlessly <em>bolt</em> listeners onto events. Minimize boilerplate to post messages, forming a beautiful <em>bolt</em> of conversational cloth. Leverage TypeScript to autocomplete code faster than a lighting <em>bolt</em>. Go ahead, bolt toward <a href=https://github.com/slackapi/bolt target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Bolt</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=april>April<a href=#april class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to April" title="Direct link to April" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Parent messages in a thread will no longer explicitly list their replies. Instead of a large <code>replies</code> array containing threaded message replies, we'll provide a lighter-weight list of <code>reply_users</code>, plus a <code>reply_users_count</code> and the <code>latest_reply</code> message. These new fields are already available. We'll remove the <code>replies</code> array on <strong>March 31st, 2020</strong>.</li>
<li class="">Make your app a better listener with the <code>app_home_opened</code> event. When a user enters a conversation with your app, you can trigger a friendly onboarding flow, a whimsical welcome message, or a deep-dive into dialog.</li>
<li class="">Retrieve all active incidents, rather than just the most recent one, using version 2.0.0 of the Slack Status API.</li>
<li class="">Buttons in message blocks have gained some color. Use the new <code>style</code> field to visually compel and alert users.</li>
<li class="">We're returning a more descriptive <code>limit_required</code> error when you call <code>users.list</code> or <code>channels.list</code> for teams containing tens of thousands of responses. To avoid the peril of errors entirely, use pagination.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=march>March<a href=#march class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to March" title="Direct link to March" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Taking a novel approach to pagination, the v5 release of our <a href=https://github.com/slackapi/node-slack-sdk/releases target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Slack SDK for Node.js</a> supports Node v8 LTS and above. It also splits the client into three separately installable packages optimized for speed and bundle size. Work with other languages or frameworks? Browse other tools built for you.</li>
<li class="">When querying <code>dnd.teamInfo</code>, the <code>users</code> argument is required beginning <strong>June 3, 2019</strong>. Future-proof your app by explicitly listing which <code>users</code> you wish to see <em>Do Not Disturb</em> settings for.</li>
<li class="">Harness a hint of time travel for your app. Schedule messages for delivery at the time of your choosing.</li>
<li class="">We're starting to enforce (more firmly) the 5GB file upload limit for workspaces on a Free plan. Some API endpoints will yield tombstoned files with the content redacted.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=february>February<a href=#february class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to February" title="Direct link to February" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">We're retiring the <code>files.comments.add</code> and <code>files.comments.edit</code> methods on <strong>May 22nd, 2019</strong>.</li>
<li class="">We're loosening up limits on dialogs. You can use five extra elements (ten total) and lovingly label them with longer lengths of letters.</li>
<li class="">When your exacting maths require the precise number of members party to a particular conversation, use the new <code>include_num_members</code> parameter with <code>conversations.info</code>.</li>
<li class="">Build better messages with Block Kit, a set of building blocks for messages and vast, interactive workflows. And, build messages better with Block Kit Builder.</li>
<li class="">We're limiting legacy tester tokens by revoking them when they're left unused for several months. As a pleasant counterpoint, our method testers let you bring your own token now.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=january>January<a href=#january class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to January" title="Direct link to January" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Apps endure, even when their installing user leaves the team—<em>as long as</em> the app doesn't perform actions on behalf of the installing user. This new behavior rolls out to free, paid, and Enterprise org teams over the next week.</li>
<li class="">Conversation objects associated with shared channels now feature a <code>conversation_host_id</code> field, indicating the workspace or Enterprise organization that "hosts" the shared channel.</li>
<li class="">We're erasing the <code>shares</code> attribute from "shared channel" conversation objects. In methods like <code>conversations.history</code> and the Events and RTM APIs, enjoy a lighter-weight list of the <code>shared_team_ids</code> representing the teams across which the conversation is shared.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/compilation>Compilation</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2019/09/01/what-they-see-is-what-you-get-and-more-and-less>What you see is what you get and more and less</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2019-09-01T00:00:00.000Z>September 1, 2019</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>This autumn, Slack will make what-you-see-is-what-you-get (WYSIWYG) editing available to users.</p>
<p>Once we release WYSIWYG editing, the <code>text</code> field found in message objects your app encounters will become an <em>approximation</em> of a user's more richly formatted message.</p>
<p>To capture a message's full nuance and vibrancy, your app may look to the new <code>blocks</code> attribute included with such messages.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/new-feature>New feature</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about What you see is what you get and more and less" href=/changelog/2019/09/01/what-they-see-is-what-you-get-and-more-and-less><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2019-07-deprecate-early-tls-versions>Deprecate early TLS versions</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2019-07-01T00:00:00.000Z>July 1, 2019</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>When your app, custom integration, or bot communicates with Slack via HTTP, it uses <a href=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Transport_Layer_Security target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">TLS</a> (Transport Layer Security) to ensure data privacy and integrity.</p>
<p>There are multiple major versions of TLS, including <code>v1.0</code>, <code>1.1</code>, <code>1.2</code>, and <code>1.3</code>. Versions <code>1.0</code> and <code>1.1</code> are deprecated and should no longer be used.</p>
<p>On <strong>March 4, 2020</strong>, we'll require all communications with Slack to use TLS version <code>1.2</code> or greater.</p>
<p>All TLS connections must use the <a href=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Server_Name_Indication target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">SNI extension</a>. Lastly, TLS connections must support at least one of the following supported cipher suites:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><code>ECDHE-RSA-AES128-GCM-SHA256</code></li>
<li class=""><code>ECDHE-RSA-AES256-GCM-SHA384</code></li>
<li class=""><code>ECDHE-RSA-AES128-SHA</code></li>
<li class=""><code>ECDHE-RSA-AES256-SHA</code></li>
<li class=""><code>AES128-GCM-SHA256</code></li>
<li class=""><code>AES256-GCM-SHA384</code></li>
</ul>
<p>Using TLS version <code>1.2</code> or greater makes Slack safer for everyone.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>Breaking change</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/deprecation>Deprecation</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Deprecate early TLS versions" href=/changelog/2019-07-deprecate-early-tls-versions><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2019-06-have-scim-will-paginate>Have SCIM, will paginate</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2019-06-01T00:00:00.000Z>June 1, 2019</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We're modernizing the <a class="" href=/reference/scim-api#get_users>GET /Users</a> and <a class="" href=/reference/scim-api#get_groups>GET /Groups</a> methods of our <a class="" href=/admins/scim-api>SCIM user management API</a> by putting a more reasonable upper bound on results served per page.</p>
<p>The <a href=http://www.simplecloud.info/specs/draft-scim-api-01.html#query-resources target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">SCIM spec</a> allows for pagination and these methods have long supported it, but we've accepted higher <code>count</code> values in the past.</p>
<p>The changes described below are effective <strike>July 8th, 2019</strike> <strong>August 30th, 2019</strong>.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/new-feature>New feature</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>Breaking change</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Have SCIM, will paginate" href=/changelog/2019-06-have-scim-will-paginate><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2019-03-wild-west-for-files-no-more>Wild West no more (for file limits, at least)</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2019-03-01T00:00:00.000Z>March 1, 2019</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Free teams feature a 5 GB limit on file uploads. However, as in the Wild Wild West of yore, the limit wasn't enforced. As of March 5, 2019, we're starting to enforce the file upload limit more firmly: only the last 5 GB of files will be visible to Free teams. In APIs that return file uploads, older files beyond the limit will be shown as 'tombstoned,' with redacted information and a <code>"hidden_by_limit"</code> field.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Wild West no more (for file limits, at least)" href=/changelog/2019-03-wild-west-for-files-no-more><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2019/02/01/cemented-fate-for-file-comments>Cemented fate for file comments</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2019-02-01T00:00:00.000Z>February 1, 2019</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>File threads superseded file comments in <a class="" href=/changelog/2018-05-file-threads-soon-tread>July 2018</a>. On <strong>May 22nd, 2019</strong>, we will permanently retire the <code>files.comments.add</code> and <code>files.comments.edit</code> API methods.</p>
<p>Vintage file comments remain accessible and deletable with <code>files.comments.get</code> and <code>file.comments.delete</code>.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/deprecation>Deprecation</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Cemented fate for file comments" href=/changelog/2019/02/01/cemented-fate-for-file-comments><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2018/12/31/compilation>2018 shortform changelog entries</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2018-12-31T00:00:00.000Z>December 31, 2018</time></div></header><div class=markdown><h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=december>December<a href=#december class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to December" title="Direct link to December" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Post replies in a thread with incoming webhooks: the <code>thread_ts</code> parameter now puts your webhook reply in its proper place.</li>
<li class="">The data structure of messages received from our APIs will change with the <a href=https://medium.com/slack-developer-blog/catching-up-on-all-things-spec-851f8c5136fb#df8b target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">launch of Block Kit</a> early next year. In return you'll be able to add newer, clearer visual components to make your app's messages magnificent. Even if you aren't using it, your apps may be affected by the additions.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=november>November<a href=#november class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to November" title="Direct link to November" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Apps may now restrict Web API requests to as many as <em>10</em> IP address ranges.</li>
<li class="">The developer preview for workspace apps has ended. We're taking the components of workspace apps and breaking them apart: applying them in phases to <em>existing</em> as well as new apps. <a href=https://medium.com/@SlackAPI/an-important-update-on-workspace-apps-aabc9e42a98b target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Read more about the motivation behind ending the preview</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=september>September<a href=#september class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to September" title="Direct link to September" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">As public channels become private, they now retain their original channel ID. Legacy methods like <code>groups.*</code> and <code>channels.*</code> don't support these transitional channel types and Conversations API methods must be used instead.</li>
<li class="">Whatever flavor of workspace token you're using, you can now expect the same <code>invalid_auth</code> error code when the token is invalid. You'll receive this error whether the token is expired, revoked, or just plain wrong. Use our OAuth 2.0-based token refresh system to refresh expired tokens safely.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=august>August<a href=#august class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to August" title="Direct link to August" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Workspace apps may now continuously rotate shorter-lived tokens without downtime. Our OAuth 2.0-based token refresh system is strongly recommended for all workspace apps. Expiring and rotating tokens is required for all distributed workspace apps.</li>
<li class="">Clear clever custom statuses like clockwork. Apps can add expiration dates when setting custom statuses for people.</li>
<li class="">We're postponing planned changes around scope requirements for app and bot access to email addresses. The new date is in autumn, on <strong>October 16th, 2018</strong>.</li>
<li class="">Dialogs now follow a separation of callback and state. Read more about the new <code>state</code> parameter and how it differs from <code>callback_id</code>.</li>
<li class="">Verifying requests from Slack just got easier: <a href=https://github.com/slackapi/node-slack-interactive-messages target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">our Node Interactive Messages SDK</a>, <a href=https://github.com/slackapi/node-slack-events-api target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Node Events API SDK</a>, and <a href=https://github.com/slackapi/python-slack-events-api target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Python Events API SDK</a> now verify request signatures automatically.</li>
<li class=""><em>"40k ought to be enough characters for any message."</em> - Slack Platform Gatekeepers. Messages are now limited to 40,000 characters.</li>
<li class="">Your workspace app can use the new <code>apps.uninstall</code> method to uninstall itself from a single workspace, revoking all tokens associated with it. To revoke a workspace token <em>without</em> uninstalling the app, use <code>auth.revoke</code>.</li>
<li class="">It's official: workspace apps can reach out to and converse with anyone using the new <code>conversations.app_home:create</code> scope. No more fumbling with conversation IDs or different methods: just plug the user's ID into <code>chat.postMessage</code> and go.</li>
<li class="">If your workspace app posts ghostly messages with <code>chat.postEphemeral</code>, you may have noticed a <code>no_permission</code> error thrown instead of <code>channel_not_found</code> when your app isn't a member of the target conversation. Turns out we actually <em>could</em> find the channel after all.</li>
<li class="">We updated our <a href=https://slack.com/terms-of-service/api-updated target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Slack App Developer Policy and API Terms of Service</a> to provide more detailed guidance, but we have not made material changes. The new policy is effective <strong>August 31, 2018</strong>. Together, we keep Slack a safe, private and secure platform for work.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=july>July<a href=#july class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to July" title="Direct link to July" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Pagination rules the nation and the Slack API. These methods newly support cursors: <code>files.info</code>, <code>groups.list</code>, <code>im.list</code>, <code>mpim.list</code>, <code>reactions.list</code>, and <code>stars.list</code>. For apps created after <strong>August 7, 2018</strong>, results will be returned in perfect, piecemeal pages <em>by default</em>.</li>
<li class="">With <a href=https://sdt.builtbyslack.com target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Slack developer tools</a> you can now quickly look up documentation, investigate the structure of messages, and more, all inside of Slack.</li>
<li class="">Commenting on files is now just like replying to a message.</li>
<li class="">HTTP requests originating from Slack now support Mutual TLS. Use Mutual TLS to attain the highest level of confidence that requests from Slack are, in fact, authentic. Read more.</li>
<li class="">Get ready to lend users a hand and start working on their behalf. Now workspace apps can ask for permission to read & write personalized settings like reminders, custom status, and profile data.</li>
<li class="">Our recently launched message actions are now available for use in all Enterprise organization workspaces and any Shared Channels within them.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=june>June<a href=#june class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to June" title="Direct link to June" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Confidently verify a request originates from Slack by validating our new request signatures. The signing process replaces the use of verification tokens, now deprecated.</li>
<li class="">We expect file threads to arrive after <strong>July 19, 2018</strong>. Do you manage a Slack app relying heavily on files or file comments? Join our <em>pilot program</em> and prepare your app for file threads ahead of the transition.</li>
<li class="">Learn when private channels are deleted with the new <code>group_deleted</code> event, now available for the Events and RTM APIs.</li>
<li class="">The Conversations API now supports workspace apps, using three simplified scopes: <code>conversations:history</code>, <code>conversations:read</code>, and <code>conversations:write</code>. We recommend upgrading your apps in developer preview to the Conversations API as soon as possible.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=may>May<a href=#may class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to May" title="Direct link to May" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Beginning <strong>October 16, 2018</strong> the <code>users:read.email</code> scope is <em>required</em> to retrieve the <code>email</code> field from user profiles while using <em>user</em> or <em>workspace</em> tokens. Consult our previous announcements on this topic from 2016 and 2017 for migration tips and some historical perspective.</li>
<li class="">Adding contextual actions lets users send specific messages to your app at will. <a href=https://medium.com/@SlackAPI/introducing-actions-a-simple-shortcut-attached-to-every-slack-message-e2404414ece target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Here are some amazing things</a> our partners do with actions. This blueprint demonstrates the ineffable <em>synergy</em> of using actions and dialogs together.</li>
<li class="">We're compiling a <a href=https://github.com/slackapi/slack-api-specs/tree/master/events-api target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">humble library of JSON schema</a> about the Events API into a kind of <a href=https://github.com/slackapi/slack-api-specs target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">open specification</a> called <a href=https://www.asyncapi.com/ target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">AsyncAPI</a>.</li>
<li class="">Newly-issued bot user token strings are a little longer than before. Building for the ages? Plan for token strings containing up to 255 characters.</li>
<li class="">Apps participating in our developer preview using the Events API will need to subscribe to <code>message.app_home</code> events for a focused feed of messages between your app and the people who interface with them through the <em>app home</em>. These messages aren't delivered to <code>message.im</code> subscriptions now.</li>
<li class="">File threads, a replacement for file comments, is on the way!</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=april>April<a href=#april class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to April" title="Direct link to April" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Measure drop off and send helpful follow ups when users cancel dialogs with these opt-in cancellation notifications.</li>
<li class="">Have a bot user token you don't need or want to use anymore? Now you can use <code>xoxb-</code> tokens with <code>auth.revoke</code>.</li>
<li class="">Your workspace token-based apps in <em>developer preview</em> must now request the <code>files:write</code> scope to upload & manage files instead of <code>files:write:user</code>. Existing access grants are backfilled. Know your read & write rights.</li>
<li class="">Working with workspace token-based apps as part of our preview? Please start using <code>oauth.access</code> instead of <code>oauth.token</code> during installation.</li>
<li class="">Some bots are users too. Now you can find a bot user's <code>user_id</code> with <code>bots.info</code>.</li>
<li class="">Enhance your dialogs with dynamic form elements "borrowed" from message menus.</li>
<li class="">Rediscover the conversations you're party to with <code>users.conversations</code>.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=march>March<a href=#march class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to March" title="Direct link to March" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">We corrected and clarified the behavior of <code>users.profile.set</code> to only allow <em>admins</em> of paid teams to update email address profile fields.</li>
<li class="">We added a <code>type</code> field to the requests dispatched to your <em>Options Load URL</em>, used in message menus and— well, it doesn't work anywhere else <em>yet</em> but we'll have a dialog about that one day...</li>
<li class="">This significant upgrade to the <a href=https://github.com/slackapi/node-slack-sdk/releases/tag/v4.0.0 target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Slack SDK for Node.js</a> modernizes one of the most widely-used JavaScript libraries on our platform with strong typing, more intuitive method signatures, and comfortingly predictable release cycles. It also sheds its aging DataStore, which has not evolved in tandem with the realities of building apps for today's workspaces. Learn more about upgrading in <a href=https://medium.com/slack-developer-blog/noteworthy-updates-to-the-slack-node-sdk-d3f77389d6c7 target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">our announcement</a>.</li>
<li class="">We are continuing to decrease the maximum number of results returned by <code>members</code> arrays returned in <code>channels.*</code> and <code>rtm.start</code>, with the limit currently set to 500 results. <code>conversations.members</code> provides paginated access instead. Read this announcement for detail.</li>
<li class="">Web API methods will be enhanced with tiered rate limiting beginning <strong>March 7, 2018</strong>, with most methods gaining greater limits than ever before.</li>
<li class="">Now you can follow up after users submit your dialogs. Use the new <code>response_url</code> attached to any <code>dialog_submission</code> to send messages after submission.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=february>February<a href=#february class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to February" title="Direct link to February" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Now users can respond to dialog textarea elements with up to 3,000 riveting, carefully-chosen characters.</li>
<li class="">Events API rate limiting has matured, now allowing apps up to 30,000 event deliveries per workspace per hour. Having trouble keeping up? Event deliveries will only be disabled when apps drop below a 5% successful response rate.</li>
<li class="">The <code>users.setActive</code> method was recently rendered irrelevant by our efforts to modernize our message servers. Use <code>users.setPresence</code> and/or connect via RTM to proclaim a user's presence instead. We'll remove this no-op method entirely on <strong>May 8, 2018</strong>.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=january>January<a href=#january class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to January" title="Direct link to January" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Catch up on recent changes to presence in the RTM and Web APIs and changes to come, including the deprecation of <code>users.list</code>'s <code>presence</code> parameter.</li>
<li class="">Having trouble connecting to the RTM API lately? WebSocket URIs may contain querystring parameters & some libraries don't like that. Find out more.</li>
<li class="">Workspace token apps in <em>developer preview</em> now must request the <code>chat:write</code> scope to post messages. Existing access grants are backfilled.</li>
<li class="">Active listening made easier: Subscribe to <code>app_mention</code> events to exclusively receive messages mentioning your app or bot.</li>
<li class="">Now shared channels can be made private and the implications are well worth considering, especially if assuming channel IDs beginning with C are public.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class=col><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/compilation>Compilation</a></ul></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2018/12/01/a-bric-a-brac-of-broadcasts-built-with-blocks>A bric a brac of broadcasts built with blocks</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2018-12-01T00:00:00.000Z>December 1, 2018</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>The data structure that represents a message now contains additional new fields on top of all <a class="" href=/reference/events/message>the existing fields</a> your app may be currently expecting. The new structure took effect on February 13, 2019.</p>
<p>These changes come with Block Kit—a new set of components for Slack apps that can be combined to create visually rich and compellingly interactive messages. You can read more about Block Kit <a href=#block-preview class="">below</a>.</p>
<p>Even if you aren't using Block Kit to compose messages, its launch still affects the data structure of messages <em>received</em> via our APIs, so read on to learn how to prepare your apps.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/new-feature>New feature</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>Breaking change</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about A bric a brac of broadcasts built with blocks" href=/changelog/2018/12/01/a-bric-a-brac-of-broadcasts-built-with-blocks><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2018/09/01/more-reasons-to-be-a-conversations-api-convert>More reasons to be a conversations API convert</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2018-09-01T00:00:00.000Z>September 1, 2018</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Unless your app uses the Conversations API, you'll encounter unusual results working with more exotic channel types, like shared channels and those channels converted from public to private.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>Breaking change</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about More reasons to be a conversations API convert" href=/changelog/2018/09/01/more-reasons-to-be-a-conversations-api-convert><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2018/08/01/updated-developer-policy>Developer policy updates</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2018-08-01T00:00:00.000Z>August 1, 2018</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>On August 31, 2018 we'll <a class="" href=/developer-policy>update</a> the <a class="" href=/developer-policy>Slack Application Developer Policy</a> and <a href=https://slack.com/terms-of-service/api-updated target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">API Terms of Service</a> to clarify existing guidelines that keep Slack a safe and secure platform for work.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Developer policy updates" href=/changelog/2018/08/01/updated-developer-policy><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2018/08/01/workspace-token-rotation>Workspace token rotation</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2018-08-01T00:00:00.000Z>August 1, 2018</time></div></header><div class=markdown><div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-danger admonition_xJq3 alert alert--danger"><div class=admonitionHeading_Gvgb><span class=admonitionIcon_Rf37><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule=evenodd d="M5.05.31c.81 2.17.41 3.38-.52 4.31C3.55 5.67 1.98 6.45.9 7.98c-1.45 2.05-1.7 6.53 3.53 7.7-2.2-1.16-2.67-4.52-.3-6.61-.61 2.03.53 3.33 1.94 2.86 1.39-.47 2.3.53 2.27 1.67-.02.78-.31 1.44-1.13 1.81 3.42-.59 4.78-3.42 4.78-5.56 0-2.84-2.53-3.22-1.25-5.61-1.52.13-2.03 1.13-1.89 2.75.09 1.08-1.02 1.8-1.86 1.33-.67-.41-.66-1.19-.06-1.78C8.18 5.31 8.68 2.45 5.05.32L5.03.3l.02.01z"/></svg></span>Workspace apps are deprecated</div><div class=admonitionContent_BuS1><p><a class="" href=/changelog/2021-01-workspace-apps-retiring-the-platform-graveyard-in-aug-2021>Learn more</a>.</div></div>
<p>Workspace apps use an <strong>access token</strong> to represent all the permissions granted to your app by a workspace.</p>
<p>Workspace tokens are so potent and powerful that apps should take great care to keep them safe and secret. We're releasing a OAuth 2.0-based token expiration and rotation system that will make workspace tokens short-lived while providing your app a secure means to refresh tokens as needed.</p>
<p>For more detail on the ins and outs of token rotation, check out our <a class="" href=/changelog/2021-01-workspace-apps-retiring-the-platform-graveyard-in-aug-2021>full documentation</a>.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/new-feature>New feature</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Workspace token rotation" href=/changelog/2018/08/01/workspace-token-rotation><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2018/06/01/conversations-apis-and-scopes-for-workspace-apps>Conversations APIs and scopes for workspace apps</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2018-06-01T00:00:00.000Z>June 1, 2018</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Workspace apps can now use a simplified interface for working with the <a class="" href=/apis/web-api/using-the-conversations-api>Conversations API methods</a>. A workspace app can request three new scopes: <code>conversations:history</code>, <code>conversations:read</code>, and <code>conversations:write</code>.  These three scopes cast an umbrella of permission over each different conversation type: channels, DMs, or anything in between.</p>
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-danger admonition_xJq3 alert alert--danger"><div class=admonitionHeading_Gvgb><span class=admonitionIcon_Rf37><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule=evenodd d="M5.05.31c.81 2.17.41 3.38-.52 4.31C3.55 5.67 1.98 6.45.9 7.98c-1.45 2.05-1.7 6.53 3.53 7.7-2.2-1.16-2.67-4.52-.3-6.61-.61 2.03.53 3.33 1.94 2.86 1.39-.47 2.3.53 2.27 1.67-.02.78-.31 1.44-1.13 1.81 3.42-.59 4.78-3.42 4.78-5.56 0-2.84-2.53-3.22-1.25-5.61-1.52.13-2.03 1.13-1.89 2.75.09 1.08-1.02 1.8-1.86 1.33-.67-.41-.66-1.19-.06-1.78C8.18 5.31 8.68 2.45 5.05.32L5.03.3l.02.01z"/></svg></span>Workspace apps are deprecated</div><div class=admonitionContent_BuS1><p><a class="" href=/changelog/2021-01-workspace-apps-retiring-the-platform-graveyard-in-aug-2021>Learn more</a>.</div></div>
<p>These new scopes make it even easier to use <a class="" href=/apis/web-api/using-the-conversations-api>Conversations API methods</a>, allowing apps to negotiate permissions for, and then interact with, all types of conversations at once.</p>
<p><img decoding=async loading=lazy alt="The latest and greatest conversations scopes" src=/assets/images/conversations_scopes-172c945056bcb138d1a63f8897b7d247.png width=1422 height=454 class=img_ev3q /></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/new-feature>New feature</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Conversations APIs and scopes for workspace apps" href=/changelog/2018/06/01/conversations-apis-and-scopes-for-workspace-apps><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2018/05/01/app-home-events-for-workspace-apps>App home events for workspace apps</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2018-05-01T00:00:00.000Z>May 1, 2018</time></div></header><div class=markdown><div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-danger admonition_xJq3 alert alert--danger"><div class=admonitionHeading_Gvgb><span class=admonitionIcon_Rf37><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule=evenodd d="M5.05.31c.81 2.17.41 3.38-.52 4.31C3.55 5.67 1.98 6.45.9 7.98c-1.45 2.05-1.7 6.53 3.53 7.7-2.2-1.16-2.67-4.52-.3-6.61-.61 2.03.53 3.33 1.94 2.86 1.39-.47 2.3.53 2.27 1.67-.02.78-.31 1.44-1.13 1.81 3.42-.59 4.78-3.42 4.78-5.56 0-2.84-2.53-3.22-1.25-5.61-1.52.13-2.03 1.13-1.89 2.75.09 1.08-1.02 1.8-1.86 1.33-.67-.41-.66-1.19-.06-1.78C8.18 5.31 8.68 2.45 5.05.32L5.03.3l.02.01z"/></svg></span>Workspace apps are deprecated</div><div class=admonitionContent_BuS1><p><a class="" href=/changelog/2021-01-workspace-apps-retiring-the-platform-graveyard-in-aug-2021>Learn more</a>.</div></div>
<p>We've added the <a class="" href=/reference/events/message.app_home><code>message.app_home</code></a> event for workspace apps building on our <a class="" href=/changelog/2021-01-workspace-apps-retiring-the-platform-graveyard-in-aug-2021>developer preview</a>.</p>
<p>If you subscribe to <a class="" href=/reference/events/message.im><code>message.im</code></a> events to receive messages between users and your app in the special kinds of 1:1 conversations had in your <em>app homes</em>, you <strong>must</strong> add a subscription to <code>message.app_home</code> to continue receiving and acting on those messages.</p>
<p>Workspace apps grant apps a dedicated space within Slack where members can interact directly— we call it your <strong><em>App Home</em></strong>. Apps can use this space for personal notifications, onboarding information, and other helpful features.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>Breaking change</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about App home events for workspace apps" href=/changelog/2018/05/01/app-home-events-for-workspace-apps><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2018-05-file-threads-soon-tread>File threads soon tread</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2018-05-01T00:00:00.000Z>May 1, 2018</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We're fixing file comments and in the process we're phasing out some related API methods and events.</p>
<p>File comments look like messages in a channel but they <em>aren't</em>. They travel with files, wherever shared, disrupting conversation at inopportune moments.</p>
<p>We started to gradually roll out <em>file threads</em> on July 23, 2018. Sharing a file with a channel will now create an actual message instead of something that looked convincingly <em>like</em> a message. People and bots may reply to that message as they would any other message. You can even upload files <em>into</em> threads.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>Breaking change</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/deprecation>Deprecation</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about File threads soon tread" href=/changelog/2018-05-file-threads-soon-tread><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2018/04/01/oauth-flow-changes-for-workspace-token-preview-apps>OAuth flow changes for workspace token preview apps</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2018-04-01T00:00:00.000Z>April 1, 2018</time></div></header><div class=markdown><div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-danger admonition_xJq3 alert alert--danger"><div class=admonitionHeading_Gvgb><span class=admonitionIcon_Rf37><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule=evenodd d="M5.05.31c.81 2.17.41 3.38-.52 4.31C3.55 5.67 1.98 6.45.9 7.98c-1.45 2.05-1.7 6.53 3.53 7.7-2.2-1.16-2.67-4.52-.3-6.61-.61 2.03.53 3.33 1.94 2.86 1.39-.47 2.3.53 2.27 1.67-.02.78-.31 1.44-1.13 1.81 3.42-.59 4.78-3.42 4.78-5.56 0-2.84-2.53-3.22-1.25-5.61-1.52.13-2.03 1.13-1.89 2.75.09 1.08-1.02 1.8-1.86 1.33-.67-.41-.66-1.19-.06-1.78C8.18 5.31 8.68 2.45 5.05.32L5.03.3l.02.01z"/></svg></span>Workspace apps are deprecated</div><div class=admonitionContent_BuS1><p><a class="" href=/changelog/2021-01-workspace-apps-retiring-the-platform-graveyard-in-aug-2021>Learn more</a>.</div></div>
<p>We're simplifying the installation process for workspace apps.</p>
<p>Now workspace apps can and should use the <a class="" href=/reference/methods/oauth.access><code>oauth.access</code></a> method instead of <code>oauth.token</code> during the verification code exchange phase of app installation via OAuth 2.0.</p>
<p>When used with workspace apps, the response for <code>oauth.access</code> morphs into a response similar to that of <code>oauth.token</code>, but with a few improvements detailed <a href=#token_acess class="">below</a>.</p>
<p>Now <a class="" href=/reference/methods/oauth.access><code>oauth.access</code></a> may be used by workspace apps instead of <code>oauth.token</code>, simplifying a common hurdle when getting started with workspace apps.</p>
<p>Finally, we're replacing <code>apps.permissions.info</code> with <code>apps.permissions.scopes.list</code> and <code>apps.permissions.resources.list</code>.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>Breaking change</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about OAuth flow changes for workspace token preview apps" href=/changelog/2018/04/01/oauth-flow-changes-for-workspace-token-preview-apps><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2018/04/01/scoping-file-rights-for-writes-in-workspace-token-apps>Scoping file rights for writes in workspace token apps</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2018-04-01T00:00:00.000Z>April 1, 2018</time></div></header><div class=markdown><div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-danger admonition_xJq3 alert alert--danger"><div class=admonitionHeading_Gvgb><span class=admonitionIcon_Rf37><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule=evenodd d="M5.05.31c.81 2.17.41 3.38-.52 4.31C3.55 5.67 1.98 6.45.9 7.98c-1.45 2.05-1.7 6.53 3.53 7.7-2.2-1.16-2.67-4.52-.3-6.61-.61 2.03.53 3.33 1.94 2.86 1.39-.47 2.3.53 2.27 1.67-.02.78-.31 1.44-1.13 1.81 3.42-.59 4.78-3.42 4.78-5.56 0-2.84-2.53-3.22-1.25-5.61-1.52.13-2.03 1.13-1.89 2.75.09 1.08-1.02 1.8-1.86 1.33-.67-.41-.66-1.19-.06-1.78C8.18 5.31 8.68 2.45 5.05.32L5.03.3l.02.01z"/></svg></span>Workspace apps are deprecated</div><div class=admonitionContent_BuS1><p><a class="" href=/changelog/2021-01-workspace-apps-retiring-the-platform-graveyard-in-aug-2021>Learn more</a>.</div></div>
<p>We're simplifying some permission scopes as part of the workspace apps developer preview.</p>
<p>Beginning today, workspace apps must request <a class="" href=/reference/scopes/files.write><code>files:write</code></a> instead of <code>files:write:user</code> during installation or when seeking elevated permissions.</p>
<p>Now <code>files:write</code> represents your app's ability to upload and manage files.</p>
<p>Experiencing <em>déjà vu</em>? This is just like <a class="" href=/changelog/2018-01-the-right-chat-write-for-workspace-token-apps>that time</a> we did this for <code>chat:write</code>.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>Breaking change</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>announcement</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Scoping file rights for writes in workspace token apps" href=/changelog/2018/04/01/scoping-file-rights-for-writes-in-workspace-token-apps><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2018-truncating-really-long-messages>Truncating really long messages</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2018-04-01T00:00:00.000Z>April 1, 2018</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We're tidying up the character limits on the <code>text</code> field of posted messages.</p>
<p>Beginning April 25th, 2018, we truncated messages sent to Slack that are longer than 500,000 characters. As of July 12, 2018, we truncate at 100,000 characters.</p>
<p>Over the <a href=#when class="">next several weeks</a>, we slowly lowered the allowed character count.</p>
<p>On <strong>August 12, 2018</strong> we started truncating messages containing more than <strong>40,000 characters</strong>.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Truncating really long messages" href=/changelog/2018-truncating-really-long-messages><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2018/03/01/great-rate-limits>Great rate limits</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2018-03-01T00:00:00.000Z>March 1, 2018</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>Until now, the <a class="" href=/apis/web-api/rate-limits>rate limits</a> governing the <a class="" href=/apis/web-api/>Slack Web API</a> have been vague, even sometimes undefined.</p>
<p>This week we are rolling out an evolved rate limiting system granting a greater number of requests to most <a class="" href=/reference/methods>methods</a> and sets responsible defaults in the few cases where limits were more mysterious or unenforced.</p>
<p>We've granted a brief grace period to a small number of apps & integrations to adjust.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Great rate limits" href=/changelog/2018/03/01/great-rate-limits><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2018-01-presence-present-and-future>Presence present and future</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2018-01-30T00:00:00.000Z>January 30, 2018</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>The RTM API's <code>presence_change</code> event is now <strong>only</strong> available via <a class="" href=/apis/web-api/user-presence-and-status#subscriptions>presence subscriptions</a> and <a class="" href=/reference/methods/rtm.start><code>rtm.start</code></a> <strong>no longer</strong> includes user presence status in its response.</p>
<p>We incrementally announced these changes in <a class="" href=/changelog/2017-06-batch-presence-and-presence-subscriptions>June</a> and <a class="" href=/changelog/2017-10-making-rtm-presence-subscription-only>October</a> 2017.</p>
<p>Today, we're <em>also</em> announcing the <strong>deprecation</strong> of the optional <code>presence</code> parameter in <a class="" href=/reference/methods/users.list><code>users.list</code></a>. Beginning <strong>September 26th, 2018</strong>, the <code>presence</code> parameter and corresponding fields will no longer be available from <code>users.list</code>.</p>
<p>Developers utilizing user presence state in their applications and integrations should review this guide to the many recent and coming changes to presence.</p>
<p>Update: <a class="" href=/reference/methods/users.setActive><code>users.setActive</code></a> is also deprecated due to underlying functionality not being available in our most modern message servers.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>Breaking change</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Presence present and future" href=/changelog/2018-01-presence-present-and-future><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2018/01/11/dont-let-websocket-uris-with-query-strings-get-you-down>Don't let websocket URIs with query strings get you down</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2018-01-11T00:00:00.000Z>January 11, 2018</time></div></header><div class=markdown><p>We now serve query string parameters on the <code>wss://</code> WebSocket URIs produced by <a class="" href=/reference/methods/rtm.connect><code>rtm.connect</code></a> and <a class="" href=/reference/methods/rtm.start><code>rtm.start</code></a>.</p>
<p>While the specification for WebSockets explicitly allows query string parameters, some third party libraries not fully implementing the spec may handle these parameters incorrectly, stripping them off and invalidating your attempts to open a connection.</p>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=known-issues>Known issues<a href=#known-issues class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to Known issues" title="Direct link to Known issues" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<p>Though we didn't anticipate issues sending query strings in websocket URIs, some libraries and frameworks may need tinkering with.</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Use <a href=https://github.com/nlopes/slack target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class=""><strong>Slack API in Go</strong></a> AKA <code>github.com/nlopes/slack</code>? Update to the latest version of this Golang project to resolve connection issues. A <a href=https://github.com/nlopes/slack/pull/217 target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">recent commit</a> merged with master fixes websocket URI handling.</li>
</ul></div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/new-feature>New feature</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about Don't let websocket URIs with query strings get you down" href=/changelog/2018/01/11/dont-let-websocket-uris-with-query-strings-get-you-down><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2018-01-the-right-chat-write-for-workspace-token-apps>The right chat:write for workspace token apps</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2018-01-11T00:00:00.000Z>January 11, 2018</time></div></header><div class=markdown><div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-danger admonition_xJq3 alert alert--danger"><div class=admonitionHeading_Gvgb><span class=admonitionIcon_Rf37><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule=evenodd d="M5.05.31c.81 2.17.41 3.38-.52 4.31C3.55 5.67 1.98 6.45.9 7.98c-1.45 2.05-1.7 6.53 3.53 7.7-2.2-1.16-2.67-4.52-.3-6.61-.61 2.03.53 3.33 1.94 2.86 1.39-.47 2.3.53 2.27 1.67-.02.78-.31 1.44-1.13 1.81 3.42-.59 4.78-3.42 4.78-5.56 0-2.84-2.53-3.22-1.25-5.61-1.52.13-2.03 1.13-1.89 2.75.09 1.08-1.02 1.8-1.86 1.33-.67-.41-.66-1.19-.06-1.78C8.18 5.31 8.68 2.45 5.05.32L5.03.3l.02.01z"/></svg></span>Workspace apps are deprecated</div><div class=admonitionContent_BuS1><p><a class="" href=/changelog/2021-01-workspace-apps-retiring-the-platform-graveyard-in-aug-2021>Learn more</a>.</div></div>
<p>Legacy workspace apps are deprecated and will retire in August 2021. Learn more.</p>
<p>We're simplifying some permission scopes as part of the workspace apps developer preview.</p>
<p>Beginning today, workspace apps must request <a class="" href=/reference/scopes/chat.write><code>chat:write</code></a> instead of <code>chat:write:user</code> during installation or when seeking elevated permissions.</p>
<p>Now <code>chat:write</code> represents your app's ability to post messages in the channels and contexts granted to it.</div><footer class="row docusaurus-mt-lg"><div class="col col--9"><b>Tags:</b><ul class="tags_jXut padding--none margin-left--sm"><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/breaking-change>Breaking change</a><li class=tag_QGVx><a rel=tag class="tag_zVej tagRegular_sFm0" href=/changelog/tags/announcement>Announcement</a></ul></div><div class="col text--right col--3"><a aria-label="Read more about The right chat:write for workspace token apps" href=/changelog/2018-01-the-right-chat-write-for-workspace-token-apps><b>Read more</b></a></div></footer></article><article class=margin-bottom--xl><header><h2 class=title_f1Hy><a href=/changelog/2017/12/31/compilation>2017 shortform changelog entries</a></h2><div class="container_mt6G margin-vert--md"><time datetime=2017-12-31T00:00:00.000Z>December 31, 2017</time></div></header><div class=markdown><h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=december>December<a href=#december class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to December" title="Direct link to December" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">For those moments when your app knows a user's email address but hasn't met them on Slack yet: now apps with <code>users:read.email</code> can use <code>users.lookupByEmail</code> and skip wading through <code>users.list</code>.</li>
<li class="">Turn your links into buttons by adding link buttons to your messages.</li>
<li class="">Storyboard, mock, and play make believe with these useful design templates starring your favorite platform features.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=november>November<a href=#november class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to November" title="Direct link to November" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Use <code>chat.getPermalink</code> to easily exchange a message <code>ts</code> for a permalink URL.</li>
<li class="">Why couldn't bot users use <code>bots.info</code>? We don't know but now they can too.</li>
<li class="">Help people get back to work by deep linking to your Slack app or directly to a channel.</li>
<li class="">When a workspace migrates to an Enterprise organization, existing users are given a second <em>global</em> user ID. Now you can bulk convert those with <code>migration.exchange</code> and turn off your app's translation layer, living the dream of one user ID per user.</li>
<li class="">Do what you like with this OpenAPI 2.0 specification of our Web API. Most methods now contain more helpful response examples. More specs and coverage on the way. <a href=https://medium.com/slack-developer-blog/standard-practice-slack-web-openapi-spec-daaad18c7f8 target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Read on</a> about our API spec.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=october>October<a href=#october class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to October" title="Direct link to October" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Send JSON when posting to Web API write methods. Gone are the days of perfunctory errors when sending lovingly crafted JSON to <code>chat.postMessage</code> and other methods.</li>
<li class="">We broadened support for presenting your tokens as a "bearer token" in <code>Authorization</code> HTTP headers with the Web API.</li>
<li class="">We removed the <code>latest</code>, <code>unread_count</code>, and <code>unread_count_display</code> fields from limited contexts of the new Conversations API. They weren't really supposed to be there. You won't find them spuriously lurking in the shadows again. We don't anticipate any issues but let us know if you find any.</li>
<li class="">The <code>members</code> array found in many API methods is now truncated. We continue to lower the maximum results returned. Please use <code>conversations.members</code> to manage memberships instead.</li>
<li class="">Scheduled changes and feature retirements to the Slack platform are now easier to find in our forward-looking calendar of upcoming changes.</li>
<li class="">The RTM API's <code>presence_change</code> event requires <code>presence_sub</code> subscriptions beginning <strong>November 15, 2017</strong>.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=september>September<a href=#september class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to September" title="Direct link to September" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Ask users for more structured form-based information with Dialogs.</li>
<li class="">Now you can customize your app's experience by the locale and language preferred by users, channels, and other conversational constructs. Start practicing your Klingon. 🖖</li>
<li class="">Shared Channels let Slack apps collaborate with users across different organizations.</li>
<li class="">The Conversations API is a collection of more than 15 Web API methods normalizing the way apps deal with channels, direct messages, and more. Never rely on the first character of a channel ID again.</li>
<li class="">The role of <code>@username</code> is changing on the platform but we're making the transition as backwards-compatible as possible.</li>
<li class="">We are clarifying two terms encountered throughout Slack, <em>"team"</em> (the people you <em>talk</em> to in Slack) and <em>"workspace"</em> (the place you do work). You'll find many <em>team</em> references updated to <em>workspace</em> across Slack and API documentation. With artifacts like the <code>team</code> object, field, and parameters scattered through the platform, you'll often still encounter <code>team</code> while reading and programming.</li>
<li class="">No more sad panda 🐼 because we fixed it — Now the outgoing webhook response payload includes a <code>thread_ts</code> attribute so you know if the message is triggered in a thread!</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=august>August<a href=#august class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to August" title="Direct link to August" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Batten down the hatches! Further secure your internal integrations by restricting token use of Web API methods to specific IP addresses you trust: IP allowlisting is here.</li>
<li class="">Improve your custom unfurling flows with enhancements to authenticated unfurls and <code>chat.unfurl</code>.</li>
<li class="">No longer the sole domain of slash commands and interactive messages, now apps can emit their own ghostly ephemeral messages with <code>chat.postEphemeral</code>.</li>
<li class=""><em>Temporary rollback</em>: We've reinstated access to the <code>email</code> attribute for bot and user tokens. On <strong>August 1, 2017</strong> we proceeded with limiting email access to user tokens with <code>users:read.email</code>.</li>
<li class="">Our developer preview for a new kind of Slack app based on workspace tokens is <em>open</em>. Learn how to work with workspace tokens and about our new Permissions API. Our <a href=https://medium.com/slack-developer-blog/looking-to-the-future-of-apps-in-slack-c2633df0bcb7 target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">announcement</a> covers the story behind the token.</li>
<li class="">With so many token types decorating our platform, this guide to token types has become a necessity.</li>
<li class="">Now we allow you to learn more about OAuth permission scopes and methods, events, and token types each supports with this helpful OAuth scope library.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=july>July<a href=#july class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to July" title="Direct link to July" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Shuttle Slack app installers to the installation flow more swiftly from the Slack Marketplace with a Direct Install URL.</li>
<li class="">Our little changelog has its own RSS feed now.</li>
<li class="">Buried somewhere in this RTM announcement, we told you about the <code>latest</code> field departing from channel objects returned in the long <code>rtm.start</code> preamble. Those fields are gone. Turns out we also removed <code>unread_count_display</code> and <code>unread_count</code> too. If you're suffering from a sense of loss over these unread count fields, please drop us a line. You can still find them in <code>conversations.info</code>.</li>
<li class="">Your app has a home in Slack. <a href=https://medium.com/slack-developer-blog/giving-apps-a-new-home-in-slack-daa2ba3a75ed target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">Read all about it</a>!</li>
<li class="">Teams now have the option to limit Slack app installation <em>only</em> to apps listed in the Slack Marketplace.</li>
<li class="">We're introducing a unified cursor-based pagination model to many of our Web API methods beginning with but one: now you can drink from <code>users.list</code> one delicious sip at a time.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=june>June<a href=#june class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to June" title="Direct link to June" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Get an event when more members join your User Group or when — uh-oh, it loses members with <code>subteam_members_changed</code>.</li>
<li class="">Do you work with <code>presence_change</code> events in the RTM API? Learn about new ways to subscribe and consolidate presence events here.</li>
<li class="">We've compiled a collection of Best Practices around building fantastic Slack app user experiences. Your users will be stoked!</li>
<li class="">We've turned a light on for you and your development team: App Blueprints are like recipes for building the internal integrations your team needs to succeed.</li>
<li class="">We've corrected a long-standing bug where user or <code>@channel</code>-type mentions in back-tick fenced code blocks would trigger notifications. They won't now.</li>
<li class="">We've made very minor improvements to our OAuth-based installation process. You may notice a shifted pixel here and there but no app-facing functionality has changed.</li>
<li class="">Just like subscribing to your app's own newsletter: App Events tell the story of your app's lifecycle. Learn when your app is uninstalled with <code>app_uninstalled</code>, or when user and bot tokens are revoked with <code>tokens_revoked</code>. Pause and resume activity when teams migrate to an Enterprise organization with <code>grid_migration_started</code> and <code>grid_migration_finished</code>.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=may>May<a href=#may class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to May" title="Direct link to May" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">We <em>undocumented</em> the mysterious <code>user_id_mapping_old_to_new</code> field described in the Enterprise organization documentation. It doesn't actually exist and never has, oops!</li>
<li class="">Slackbot wants to help spread the word about your cool Slack app. Add a little HTML to your site and we'll suggest your app when your links are mentioned.</li>
<li class="">You'll soon see fewer <code>message.channel_join</code> and <code>message.channel_leave</code> message subtype events in the Events API and RTM API. Instead, you'll find these new refreshingly direct and informative events: <code>member_joined_channel</code> and <code>member_left_channel</code>.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=april>April<a href=#april class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to April" title="Direct link to April" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">The old <code>channels.list</code> API method has a new parameter: <code>exclude_members</code>. Some teams are so big and some channels have so many members that listing them all in a single API response along with every other channel is just outright impractical. Cull unneeded data easily accessed with <code>conversations.info</code> by excluding <code>members</code> fields.</li>
<li class="">We'd like you to stop using <code>rtm.start</code> and start using <code>rtm.connect</code> instead. <code>rtm.connect</code> boots quickly and works well with the most gigantic teams and enterprises of the galaxy.</li>
<li class="">It's spring cleaning time for email. We're winding down the grandfathering introduced for apps using <code>users:read</code> created before <strong>January 4th, 2017</strong>. After <strong>August 1st, 2017</strong> your apps must request <code>users:read.email</code> to gain that access. See this post for more detail. This retirement has been delayed with no date yet rescheduled.</li>
<li class="">Observe the custom status of team members with <code>users.profile.get</code>. Update a user's custom status with <code>users.profile.set</code>.</li>
<li class="">More ways to make messages interactive than before: introducing message menus. Define your options statically, dynamically, even <em>personally</em> — or use our handy conversation, channel, and user pickers. Don't forget your field guide.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=march>March<a href=#march class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to March" title="Direct link to March" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">As with the humans operating them, user objects change over time. With the new <code>updated</code> field, decisively learn last time a user object transformed. Look for it in methods including (but not limited to) <code>users.list</code> and <code>users.info</code>. It's an integer value depicting <a href=https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Unix_time target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">seconds since the epoch</a>.</li>
<li class="">We're introducing new, multimedia ways for bots and apps to express themselves in the Slack Marketplace. Follow our new guidelines to make a great impression with potential installers.</li>
<li class="">Provide users posting links with all the context and interactivity they need, right in Slack. Introducing Slack app unfurling. Here's the <a href=https://medium.com/@SlackAPI/ebcad7c531f0#.dp0ehltqg target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">announcement</a>!</li>
<li class="">Beginning <strong>March 9, 2017</strong>, events transmitted via the Events API will include <code>event_id</code> and <code>event_time</code> fields. <code>event_id</code> is globally unique across all teams while the <code>event_time</code> is when the event dispatched, in integer-based epoch time. Use these fields as you like, but there's nothing you need to do to prepare for this eventuality.</li>
<li class="">We made it easier to create and manage your Slack apps. And if you're building internal integrations for your own team, there's a better way to install your app without worrying about the OAuths. Check it out.</li>
<li class="">Looking for custom integrations? They're documented as legacy now. They still work like you're used to but we'd prefer you built your internal integrations as part of a Slack app instead.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=february>February<a href=#february class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to February" title="Direct link to February" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">Minor field changes coming to <code>channels.history</code> file messages and <code>skype</code> user profile fields.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id=january>January<a href=#january class=hash-link aria-label="Direct link to January" title="Direct link to January" translate=no>​</a></h2>
<ul>
<li class="">You have the tools and the talent — now you have the opportunity: develop for Slack Enterprise orgs. Here's <a href=https://medium.com/@SlackAPI/148185a609f2 target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">the announcement</a> for the suits.</li>
<li class="">Now your app can read, write, and party with message threads. Rolling out to teams over the next few days, message threads are a perfect place to tuck your wonderful workflows. Here's <a href=https://medium.com/@SlackAPI/cd272a42924f#.tn0geq5bf target=_blank rel="noopener noreferrer" class="">our announcement</a>.</li>
<li class="">This new year's resolution is a minor slash command revolution: a backwards-compatible, familiar, and decisive means to resolve user IDs, channel IDs, and links from references in slash command invocations.</li>
